Current Commentary

Reorganization of the American China Trading Company 30

— Yan

According to yesterday's report in the English-language *Ta Mei Wan Pao* (Greater American Evening Post), the American China Trading Company, following the United Theatres Corporation, the American-Oriental Banking Corporation, the American Eastern Trading Company, the Probst Realty Company, and the Probst Trust Company, is invoking a new law enacted in the United States due to the global economic downturn and petitioning the U.S. Court for China to allow reorganization and appoint a receiver to manage its assets. According to the company's newly appointed manager, Mr. Woodulfe, this move by the board of directors is intended to protect the interests of shareholders. As early as the beginning of March this year, the board was quite satisfied after investigating the company's financial situation. However, the current market is sluggish, and loans are difficult to recover, making it impossible to continue lending. Therefore, reorganization is the only way out. Bondholders have also been notified separately that all due interest on the company's 8% mortgage bonds and the due principal and interest on the 7% mortgage bonds will be temporarily suspended.

The American China Trading Company has been established for about 25-26 years. It was previously one of the most active players in the Shanghai real estate market, forming a near-equal triumvirate with the American Probst and the British Commercial Land Company. In past years, when Shanghai land prices soared, its annual profits were exceptionally high. The dividends received by shareholders were over 3% per week. Consequently, its stocks and bonds were closely watched by brokers in various trade associations. It developed rapidly over the years, and its capital was repeatedly increased, with bonds being issued continuously. In its current state, its paid-up capital is about 7 million yuan, and its bonds with solid guarantees are about 6 million yuan, while those without solid guarantees are about 10 million yuan. The company's total assets are about 55 million yuan. It is said that the liabilities are expected to offset the assets. However, according to our speculation, the company's book assets may be on par with its liabilities. However, with the current severe decline in real estate, it is doubtful whether the shareholders' interests can be protected and a final accounting has to be done.

Four or five years ago, the company's stocks and bonds were quite active in the market, and the stock price even exceeded double its value. Many foreign businessmen also invested in purchasing them in considerable numbers. Now that the company is under the custody of the U.S. Court for China and is beginning to reorganize, its future cannot be predicted. However, those who purchased them at high prices at the time may not be able to maintain their good value and avoid losses. The mistaken mentality of our people in blindly trusting foreign businesses in the past can now be awakened. Moreover, many Chinese who transferred their real estate deeds to American ownership had them registered through this company. They only hold a piece of paper as proof of ownership. After the reorganization, whether these Chinese deeds can be fully recovered is also a matter of concern for merchants who have dealings with the company.

League of Nations Administrative Council Resolves to Form a Thirteen-Nation Committee to Act According to Article 15 of the Covenant; The Five-Nation Committee Continues Its Task; The Italian Representative Did Not Attend the Meeting Yesterday 31

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council held two meetings this morning and unanimously passed a proposal to form a thirteen-nation committee, consisting of all members of the Administrative Council except Italy, to report on the facts of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute and make recommendations in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. The proposal was put forward by the Chairman of the Administrative Council and was initially established in a closed-door meeting, followed by a formal meeting for its passage. The Administrative Council also decided that the Five-Nation Special Committee should remain in existence to continue its mediation efforts in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant. Italian representative Aloisi did not attend either of this morning's meetings. The Thirteen-Nation Committee will hold its first meeting tomorrow. Representatives from Britain, France, Russia, Argentina, Spain, Australia, Turkey, Romania, Poland, Portugal, Denmark, Ecuador, and Chile will attend. It is noted that Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant stipulates that if the dispute cannot be resolved, the Administrative Council, by a unanimous or majority vote, shall issue a report stating the facts of the dispute and the recommendations that the Administrative Council considers fair and appropriate. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council, at its meeting this morning, decided to invoke Article 15 of the Covenant to deal with the Italian-Ethiopian dispute and to regard Italy as an aggressor. This action by the League of Nations is the result of Eden and Laval's urging yesterday that the League of Nations Administrative Council first invoke Article 15 and then implement Article 16 on sanctions. Representatives from thirteen nations attended the important meeting of the Administrative Council today. In just seventy minutes, they passed measures to apply sanctions to aggressors as stipulated in Article 15, Paragraphs 3 and 4 of the Covenant. The Italian representative was not present at the time. However, the representatives of the thirteen nations unanimously recognized that maintaining peace is the life of the League of Nations and that Italy could not be accommodated excessively. (National Telegram on the 26th)

Upon receiving the news from Geneva today that the League of Nations Administrative Council has decided to implement sanctions against Italy if Italy starts a war against Ethiopia, officials in Addis Ababa were extremely delighted. An official stated that this was what they had been hoping for and that it was gratifying that justice had finally prevailed. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

Britain, France, Russia, and Other Countries Express Firm Commitment to the Covenant; The Ethiopian Representative Attends the Meeting and Is Willing to Consider Any Recommendations 32

(Geneva) At this morning's formal public meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council, the Chairman of the Five-Nation Committee presented the Committee's report, recounting the course of seeking a peaceful resolution to the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. Although Ethiopian representative Haile Warat was not a member of the Administrative Council, he was invited by the Administrative Council and also attended this morning's meeting, stating that the Ethiopian delegation wished to reserve the right to consult with its government on any recommendations of the Administrative Council and that the Ethiopian government would give them extremely careful consideration.

The Chairman of the Administrative Council, Argentine representative Ginazu, stated that Article 15 of the Covenant had been in effect since the first meeting of the Administrative Council on September 4th. The next step is for the Administrative Council, in its capacity as a committee, to draft a report in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. As for the term of the Administrative Council, it will only end after the report of the Five-Nation Committee has been passed.

The Chairman's proposal was endorsed by British representative Eden, who stated that when the Thirteen-Nation Committee drafts the report, the governments of various countries will have the opportunity to consider within the scope of the Covenant whether a peaceful outcome can be achieved. Britain's policy has been stated responsibly, and Britain is determined to adhere to this policy. French Prime Minister Laval rose to support Eden's remarks, saying that France is willing to abide by the obligations under the Covenant to make recommendations and to carry out its duties in the spirit and letter of the Covenant, and is willing to present what it considers to be the fairest plan.

After the French Prime Minister spoke, Russian representative Litvinov rose to say that the Russian government was willing to support any resolutions made by the Administrative Council. Danish representative Munch stated that he also welcomed Chairman Ginazu's proposal to uphold the principles of the League of Nations. The Chairman's proposal was unanimously adopted by the whole meeting.

It is reported that at this morning's closed-door meeting, the representatives of Russia, Turkey, and Romania, while supporting the proposal of the Administrative Council, attached reservations to the acceptance of the report of the Five-Nation Committee, as it granted Italy too much power, which was inconsistent with the Covenant.

regarding the fact that it is in a state of activity and will not be dissolved as usual when the work is completed, should first be discussed by the General Assembly before a final decision is made (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly and the Administrative Council meetings will both adjourn from this afternoon until Saturday. However, during the adjournment period, meetings may still be convened at any time if necessary. (Havas Telegram on the 26th)

Britain, France, and Other Countries Coordinate Before the Meeting; The Administrative Council Will Not Act Hastyly If Italy and Ethiopia Do Not Engage in War 33

(Geneva) French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval, British Minister Without Portfolio Eden, Spanish representative and Chairman of the Five-Nation Subcommittee Madariaga, and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol recently jointly discussed the procedures to be adopted at tomorrow's League of Nations Administrative Council meeting for an hour before completing the process. It is generally expected that at tomorrow's Administrative Council meeting, a drafting committee will be appointed to draft the final report on the Italian-Ethiopian dispute and include the recommendations of the Administrative Council. Furthermore, the memorandum submitted by Italy to the League of Nations Administrative Council has not been considered by the Five-Nation Subcommittee, but may be studied by the drafting committee later. League of Nations officials believe that if no serious incident occurs between Italy and Ethiopia in the short term, the League of Nations Administrative Council does not intend to act hastily. After the drafting committee is established, the Administrative Council will immediately announce its adjournment, and the subcommittee will then handle routine matters. If necessary, the subcommittee may convene a meeting of the Administrative Council within 24 hours. (Havas News Agency Telegram on the 25th)

(Geneva) Today, according to the most authoritative sources here, British representative Eden and French Foreign Minister Laval have decided to request the League of Nations Administrative Council to proceed in accordance with Article 15 on Thursday to prepare for the implementation of Article 16 on sanctions against aggressor nations, and it is understood that other countries have also provisionally agreed to support the positions of Britain and France. It is also noted that the decision of the League of Nations Administrative Council this morning is not an innovation. The same procedure was also adopted in the cases of the dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia over the Gran Chaco and the dispute between China and Japan over Manchuria. Britain had also requested the invocation of Article 15 of the Covenant to deal with the Persian oil case, but the oil case was ultimately resolved through negotiations. This morning, the Administrative Council also decided that the work of the Five-Nation Committee should continue to be carried out in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant, which stipulates that the Administrative Council should make every effort to resolve the dispute. If effective, the facts and interpretations of the dispute and the terms of the resolution should be published as appropriate. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

(Geneva) As the thirteen members of the League of Nations Administrative Council, i.e., all members of the Administrative Council except Italy, discuss the recommendations under Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant, the overall situation seems to be temporarily calming down. The Administrative Council will strive to expedite everything, but with such a large group carrying out this work, it will not be as easy to achieve as the Five-Nation Special Committee, and it may have to wait for the Ethiopian government to submit a reply to the Italian government's accusations of atrocities by the Ethiopian authorities. Yesterday afternoon, the Presidium held an important meeting to discuss future procedures and decided whether the Presidium should suspend activities or elect a committee to represent all member states of the Administrative Council except Italy to draft recommendations for resolving the Italian-Ethiopian dispute in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. The Administrative Council will probably adjourn temporarily before the Committee presents its report, and the League of Nations General Assembly will also adjourn on Saturday. However, the Chairman of the General Assembly may convene a meeting at any time. There is a growing feeling that Mussolini is eager to find a "face-saving" way to withdraw his preparations for the East African war while still maintaining his position at home and internationally. (National Telegram on the 25th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Five-Nation Committee today announced the rejection of Italian representative Aloisi's "comments." Afterwards, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini called these "comments" informal in nature and therefore could not be rejected. The so-called "comments" included the following statements: "Italy considers Abyssinia a particularly dangerous enemy. Italy opposes the land adjustment proposals put forward by Britain and France, as these proposals would turn Abyssinia into a sea power and increase its danger to Italy." The "comments" also criticized the Five-Nation Committee for not allowing Italians to control the Ethiopian army. The Committee's report will be presented at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting on Thursday. French Prime Minister Laval is still striving for peace, but is greatly disappointed given Mussolini's attitude. (National News Agency Telegram on the 25th)

(London) The latest possibility in the Italian-Ethiopian situation is that Italy may demand that Abyssinia become its protectorate, but rumors that Mussolini intends to meet with French Prime Minister Laval in person to discuss this matter have now been denied by officials. The Italian newspapers expressed their views, saying that the issue of Italy's trusteeship over Abyssinia should be handled directly through negotiations between the two related countries. *Le Temps* in Paris stated that Italy wants to demand trusteeship based on Article 22 of the Covenant, as the Abyssinian people are a degenerate race. The newspaper added that it is difficult to predict how the League of Nations Administrative Council can approve this step, and it would be especially difficult for British public opinion to accept this solution. According to Article 22 of the Covenant, the right to protect degenerate races should be entrusted to advanced countries that have the resources, experience, or geographical capacity to assume this responsibility. On the eve of the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting, France still hopes to have an opportunity for reconciliation before deciding to implement sanctions. According to well-informed French observers, there will be at least a ten-day period of hesitation to strive for a mutually agreeable solution. Assuming that the first step of the League of Nations Administrative Council is to organize a committee to draft proposals, as outlined in Article 15 of the Covenant, this committee may need ten days to review everything. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

(Rome) The efforts of British, French, and Italian diplomats to mediate the Italian-Ethiopian dispute have largely failed today. Britain insists on maintaining the independence of Abyssinia, but Mussolini refuses to make this a condition for negotiations. It was learned today that Italy may request the League of Nations General Assembly to redefine the trusteeship system. This motion will definitely be strongly opposed by Britain and France, as this motion would allow Germany and other countries hoping to overthrow the post-war borders to take the opportunity. (National Telegram on the 25th)

Roosevelt Orders Publication of Embargoed Goods List, Including Six Types of Munitions, but Not Ammunition Raw Materials 36

(Washington) President Roosevelt, acting under the recently passed Neutrality Act, today ordered the prohibition of the transport of weapons and munitions to any location outside the United States. The order includes a detailed list specifying various munitions such as tanks, armored vehicles, warships, military aircraft, poison gas, etc., all defined as "war supplies." Manufacturers and vendors dealing in these items must first obtain a license before selling or transporting them. The omission of raw materials from the list has aroused widespread speculation. If European countries impose sanctions on Italy, and American businesses continue to sell raw materials to the Italian government, what will be the result? According to the Neutrality Act, the effect of this ban lasts until the end of February next year, at which time Congress will likely pass permanent neutrality measures. (25th National Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has just released the list of military supplies for which export is prohibited, as drafted by the National Munitions Control Board. This list specifies the munitions that can be embargoed to belligerent nations in wartime, and includes six categories: (1) guns, machine guns, ammunition, and tanks; (2) all types of warships; (3) assembled or disassembled aircraft and other aerial vehicles equipped with machine guns or bombs; (4) pistols and automatic pistols weighing over 630 grams; (5) aircraft and airship engines; and (6) gas and incendiary projectile launchers. Manufacturers of these munitions who intend to export their products overseas, even at this time when there is no international war, must apply to the National Munitions Control Board for a license. The Board has no right to refuse to issue licenses at this time. Raw materials used to manufacture ammunition are not included in this list. Furthermore, manufacturers and dealers of munitions must register with the National Munitions Control Board starting from November 29th. Secretary of Commerce Roper recently stated to the press that the Munitions Control Board is currently studying which raw materials and products can be included in the embargo list. (25th Havas Telegram)

(Washington) The State Department, in order to implement the wartime Neutrality Act, previously appointed a committee to study and compile a list of the types of war supplies that should be prohibited from being transported to belligerent nations in wartime. The committee's research concluded that if this ban were implemented, U.S. exports would decrease by $5 million per month in wartime. (25th Havas Telegram)

United States Speeds Up Shipbuilding, New Submarines to Be Completed Ahead of Schedule 37

It was learned today from Connecticut that the Navy Department has ordered all public and private shipyards contracted to build warships to expedite their work and has agreed to cover the expenses arising from overtime work. Two new submarines being built in Portsmouth, New Hampshire, originally scheduled to be completed in twenty-seven months, are now to be finished in fourteen months. (25th Reuters Telegram)

The Los Angeles Times of San Francisco reported today that the Japanese Navy is currently chartering merchant ships flying the Japanese flag to transport oil from San Francisco ports to Japan for storage in naval warehouses. In addition, Japanese naval oil tankers will also transport at least one million barrels from San Francisco during this period. This does not include ordinary oil purchased and transported from San Francisco by Japanese merchants. (25th Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinia Orders Border Closure, But Denies General Mobilization 41

Djibouti, Abyssinia, today closed its war zone, prohibiting foreigners from entering or exiting. This move indicates that Abyssinia believes that all parties are unable to prevent Italy from resorting to force. All routes of the Franco-Ethiopian Railway south to Ogaden and north to Danakil have been cut off by order of the Abyssinian government. Abyssinian troops in these two areas are now digging trenches under the guidance of military experts from Sweden and other countries, preparing to resist the Italian army's simultaneous attacks from Eritrea in the north and Walwal in the southeast. It is believed here that the Italian army plans to invade simultaneously from the north and south, and after meeting at the railway, join forces to directly attack the Abyssinian capital. The Abyssinian Emperor telegraphed from the capital today, reiterating his request to the League of Nations to send impartial observers to Abyssinia for investigation, but the preparations for war on both sides of the railway show that the Abyssinian Emperor no longer hopes that diplomatic means can avoid the war. A telegram from the Abyssinian capital today stated that five of the twenty male lions captured by the Abyssinian Emperor escaped from their cages, devoured one of the courtiers, and were subsequently shot dead by the machine guns of the Guards, avoiding chaos in the capital. (25th National News Agency Telegram)

The Abyssinian Emperor today reiterated his desire for peace to the League of Nations, stating that in view of the continuous provocations and to avoid unexpected incidents, he has now ordered the frontline troops to withdraw thirty miles. This order has been fully complied with. The Abyssinian Emperor also suggested to the League of Nations that it send an observer to Abyssinia so that the issue of responsibility can be determined on the spot in the event of any incidents. Rumors of an order for mobilization have recently been denied by the Abyssinian government. (25th National Telegram)

(Geneva) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol received a telegram today personally signed by the Abyssinian Emperor, arguing that if any border incidents or invasions occur in the future, a neutral observer delegation should be sent to monitor everything. The telegram stated: "Months ago, in view of Italy's attitude, provocations became increasingly serious, and if there were hostile acts, invasion could not be avoided, so a special order was issued to withdraw troops along the border by twenty kilometers to avoid conflicts and allow Italy and Britain to take the opportunity to carry out aggression. This order has been fully complied with." The telegram also recounted the Abyssinian Emperor's previous request to send impartial observers to determine the responsibility for any intrusions or acts of aggression, and asked the League of Nations Council to prepare as soon as possible what it considered necessary. The Abyssinian Emperor also firmly stated that the Abyssinian government would fully cooperate with all plans decided by the League of Nations Council. The Abyssinian Emperor also suggested that the members of the delegation should travel by plane, and the cost could be borne by the Abyssinian government. (26th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) This agency's reporter does not believe that the League of Nations will dispatch an investigation team to Abyssinia, as requested by the Abyssinian government, because dispatching an investigation team would make the current tense situation even more serious, and the geographical situation in the area where Abyssinia borders Italian colonies in East Africa is extremely complicated, and even if an investigation team is sent there, it would not be easy to fulfill its mission. (26th Havas News Agency Telegram)

Currency Stabilization, Agreement Reached Between Britain and France, Adjusting Exchange Rates to Reduce Trade Barriers, French Representative Supports British Plan 43

(Geneva) British and French representatives attending the League of Nations Economic Committee reached a compromise today on France's plan for realistic currency stabilization. The French chief representative, Bonnet, has withdrawn his proposal and instead supported the more flexible plan proposed by the British representative, Burgin, namely, that both parties reach an agreement to reduce trade barriers and reserve room for exchange rate fluctuations. Burgin also stated that all governments want to restore the international gold standard, and this can only be achieved through reciprocal treaties. Adjustments can also be made if exchange rates differ too much. It is worth noting that US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau and several other Treasury officials are currently in Europe, and the agreement reached between Britain and France today is of great importance. It is recalled that the US Treasury Secretary recently stated that the United States will not hinder other countries' efforts to stabilize their currencies. (24th National Telegram)

Britain, France, Italy, and Lithuania Discuss Memel Issue, Decide Not to Raise It at League of Nations Assembly 44

(Geneva) French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval met today with Italian representative Aloisi, British Minister without Portfolio Eden, and Austrian Foreign Minister Berger respectively. Subsequently, Laval, Aloisi, Eden, and Lithuanian Foreign Minister Lozoraitis jointly discussed the Memel issue and decided that the issue would not be raised for discussion at the League of Nations Assembly. In addition, they considered that the Lithuanian government's assurance of honest voting in the Memel autonomous parliamentary elections should be formally notified to the German government. (25th Havas News Agency Telegram)

(Berlin) The Diplomatic Political Correspondence proposes adopting a procedure similar to the Saar plebiscite in January this year, namely, that the guarantor nations of the Memel Treaty, Britain, France, Italy, and Japan, should send troops to Memel to ensure the freedom of voting in the elections this Saturday. The newspaper seems to consider the assurances made by the Lithuanian Foreign Minister to Laval and Eden in Geneva yesterday to be insufficient. (26th National Telegram)

After the dissolution of the autonomous parliament of the Memel Autonomous Region, the capital of Lithuania, it is scheduled to be re-elected on September 29 in accordance with the new election law. In view of this, the Lithuanian government, aware that Germany has issued various effective propaganda, has invited the diplomatic representatives of Britain, France, and Italy stationed in Lithuania to visit the region at that time in order to demonstrate the fairness and impartiality of this election. Tone River Rises, Major Flood Disaster in Kanto Region of Japan, Gunma Prefecture Suffers Heaviest Damage 48

(Tokyo) The unprecedented flood disaster centered on the Tone River and spreading across the Kanto Plain gradually subsided by the afternoon of the 26th, and the people in various places were slightly relieved. The important Tone Railway Bridge connecting Tokyo and the Tohoku region was spared, but the total losses in various places will reach tens of millions of yen. (26th Jiji Telegram)

Gunma (Tokyo) The losses from this heavy rain disaster were the most severe in the Gunma Prefecture. The situation as of 1:00 PM on the 26th, as far as has been ascertained, is roughly as follows: about 160 bridges washed away, 110 civilian properties washed away, 150 houses completely destroyed, 350 embankments breached, 800 prefectural highways washed away, 47 dead, 30 missing, and many injured, the actual number of whom is still unknown. It seems that the number of people drowned is likely to increase, and the number of affected households has reached 4,611. (26th Jiji Telegram)

This flood in Gunma Prefecture is the largest flood since 1910, so the Tone River area suffered the greatest losses. The 270-ken-long steel-reinforced concrete large iron bridge in Iwagami-cho, connecting Maebashi City and Gunma County, was washed away at 6:15 AM today. (26th Dentsu Telegram)

Chiba Due to the heavy rain in Chiba Prefecture, the Edogawa River rose and the embankment collapsed for 40 jō (approximately 120 meters), and muddy water flowed into the city streets, washing away 5,000 houses.

Maebashi A heavy rain disaster occurred in the Maebashi area, and the entire Shikishima Park area has become a swamp. The 600-jō-long Ōatagi Bridge was washed away at 6:00 AM on the 26th. (26th Jiji Telegram)

The Truth About the Seafarer Certification Examination 67

(Nanjing) The Shanghai Daily News' report on the seafarer certification examination is inaccurate. The Ministry of Communications is disclosing the true situation of the seafarer certification examination as follows. The Ministry of Communications' seafarer certification examination is established to ensure navigation safety and fulfill the obligations of the International Convention for the Safety of Life at Sea. Both Japan and other countries have such a system. The Ministry of Communications' seafarer certification does not restrict nationality. All foreign nationals and Japanese residents in China who serve as seafarers are treated equally. There is no discrimination between Chinese and foreign seafarers. Since the promulgation of the certification regulations, a total of 617 seafarers have applied for the examination at the Ministry of Communications. 124 Chinese seafarers failed, 14 Western seafarers failed, and 11 Japanese seafarers failed. This fact can demonstrate that there is absolutely no intention of favoring one nationality over another in the certification of seafarers. The Ministry of Communications has repeatedly extended the deadline for this examination. Recently, due to the ship schedules of some seafarers, they were unable to take the examination within the time limit. The Ministry specially took into account the situation and extended the original deadline for cracking down on uncertified seafarers, which was set for September. It is now scheduled to hold another examination simultaneously at the Shanghai, Tianjin, and Hankou Shipping Administrations from October 16 to November 10 this year. All seafarers who have taken the examination but failed and those who have not yet taken the examination can register for the examination at the local shipping administrations before the end of this month. Both navigation safety issues and seafarer livelihood issues have been taken into consideration. (26th Dispatch)

Nanchang Holds Fire Prevention Week; Citizens' Meeting Demonstrates Firefighting; The Zhendan Fire Extinguisher Performs Extremely Well 89

Nanchang Correspondence: Nanchang City's Fire Prevention Week, from the 23rd to the 27th. At 7:30 a.m. on the 21st, the Citizens' Meeting and Fire Prevention Week Opening Ceremony were held at the Provincial Stadium. More than 10,000 people attended, including leading officials from party and government agencies, representatives from industry and commerce, and citizens. The representatives stood in formation according to their designated locations. Personnel from various agencies stood in a line in front of the rostrum. Various schools and groups were arranged in a circular shape. Various performances were held in the center of the field. The temporary buildings were set up. At 7:30, music was played to open the meeting, and the flag-raising ceremony was held. After the opening ceremony, the chairman gave a report, followed by a training speech by Inspector Miao Peicheng. Then the various fire prevention, firefighting, and rescue performances began. First, Limin Store demonstrated the effectiveness of fire extinguishing bombs. In advance, the store constructed a temporary house, which was ignited with planed wood and kerosene. Suddenly, the flames blazed, penetrating the roof. Then, fire extinguishing bombs were thrown in, but because the flames were too fierce, they did not work. After dozens more were thrown in, the fire was extinguished and then re-ignited. It was ineffective. The attendees were all dumbfounded. Later, the fire brigade injected water with a light water hose, and the fire was extinguished. Then, the Zhendan fire extinguisher performed. Planed wood and kerosene were used to ignite a wooden house, and the flames rose fiercely. The manager of Xin Factory used a Zhendan machine to inject foam at the head of the fire. Although the fire was fierce, it was extinguished immediately. The audience on both sides applauded and cheered. In order to strengthen the public's confidence, the manager continued to perform once, and the results were the same as before. Finally, the Provincial Public Security Bureau's Fire Brigade performed a disguised performance, divided into four acts: (1) Gambling leads to a fire; (2) Carelessly throwing cigarette butts leads to a fire; (3) Mosquito incense touching the ground leads to a fire; (4) Careless cooking leads to a fire. Among them, the fourth act, careless cooking, ignited the entire house. Suddenly, fire trucks, water hoses, and firefighters rushed to the scene, climbing onto the roof to cut off the fire lines and injecting water separately. All kinds of scenes were like rescuing a major fire. Especially when the entire house was destroyed, thick smoke filled the air and the flames soared, making people feel frightened. Finally, the firefighters performed jumping into the safety net. They jumped from the roof into the net without any injuries. The performance ended and the meeting adjourned at about 9:00 a.m.

Measures to Reorganize Fujian Province's Finances 90

Fuzhou Correspondence: Fujian Province's local budget for the 24th year has been implemented since September. According to the budget, the annual revenue and expenditure will be short by more than one million yuan. Therefore, the Provincial Government is now strictly implementing increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. In terms of reducing expenditure, such as merging the ten administrative inspectorate commissioners' offices in the province into seven, more than 100,000 yuan can be saved annually. It is also planned to reduce the security regiment in the province to ten regiments, which can also save 200,000 to 300,000 yuan annually. The road construction project will be transferred to the county governments to be responsible for handling, and will not be paid for under the provincial appropriation. The road construction workers recruited in Zhejiang and Anhui for the various lines in northwestern Fujian will all be sent back to their hometowns. All road construction project offices will be reduced to road construction teams. The Yansha Yong Road Project Office will be changed to the First Road Construction Team, the Yonglian Road Project Office will be changed to the Second Road Construction Team, the Kanfeng Road Project Office will be changed to the Third Road Construction Team, and the Yanshunjiang Road Project Office will be changed to the Fourth Road Construction Team. The expenses saved each month are also considerable. Regarding increasing revenue, various local taxes will be strictly reorganized, with particular attention to the house and shop tax and the business tax. For bureaus and offices with large tax amounts, the Ministry of Finance plans to send personnel to supervise the collection or auditing. Because the malpractices in these two taxes are particularly deep, Weng Qingsheng, the former director of the Minhou Tax Bureau, was arrested by the Provincial Government and detained in the Security Office and the Public Security Bureau for collecting house and shop taxes from the people with white slips instead of formal donation forms. Zheng Xianlun, the former chief of the Second Section of the Ministry of Finance (currently still a inspector of the Ministry of Finance), was also arrested by the Provincial Government and detained in the Security Office and the Public Security Bureau for privately accepting subsidies from the seafood and sugar business tax bureaus, along with Huang Qinting, the director of the Seafood Tax Bureau, and Zheng Zhenfan, the director of the Sugar Tax Bureau. The authorities are currently collecting case files from all parties and will open the trial in the near future. Both the society and the political world believe that this is the most important case in the province's finances in the past ten years and are paying close attention to it. In addition, the Provincial Bank was originally scheduled to open on October 1st, and the employees of the office had all been arranged. Because the funds were not raised in time, it was postponed again. The Provincial Government has now allocated 600,000 yuan and decided to open on October 15th, and a branch office will be opened in Xiamen, and Deputy Manager Zhou Huanzhang has been sent there to prepare. After the bank is established, the Provincial Treasury will be transferred from the Central Bank to the bank for handling. The Ministry of Finance's loan of 500,000 yuan from the Central Bank has been approved by the head office and can be transferred immediately. It is agreed that 50,000 yuan will be repaid each month, with foreign rice used to offset taxes as collateral to meet urgent needs. (September 25)

Local News

Chinese Business Company to Be Reorganized; Yesterday Submitted a Request to the American Court to Appoint a Custodian; and Sent Separate Letters to Shareholders to Suspend Interest Payments 99

The American Evening Post reported that the American Chinese Business Company at 290 Sichuan Road submitted a request to the American Court in China this afternoon (26th) to appoint a custodian under Section 77B of the US Bankruptcy Act. Before the court makes a ruling, the company will continue to operate as usual. After the custodian committee is appointed, the company will be reorganized in the same way as several other companies in China, such as the United Theatre Company. According to a firm statement from the company's staff, the company's internal assets are substantial. The reason for taking this step is to view it as the most convenient way to protect the interests of those involved. The company's business includes buying, selling, and mortgaging real estate. The difficulties it has encountered are the same as those currently encountered by several other companies in Shanghai, that is, the matured funds cannot be recovered, causing the turnover to be unsustainable. All real estate companies have suffered greatly in recent months due to the impact of the recession. According to the statement, the company's capital that has been paid up totals approximately 7 million yuan, and unsecured bonds of approximately 10 million yuan and secured bonds of more than 6 million yuan have been issued. The assets and liabilities are sufficient to offset each other, totaling approximately 55 million yuan. Today, the newly appointed president and general manager, Mr. Walsh Pfeiffer, sent a circular to shareholders and holders of the company's 8% and 7% mortgage bonds, stating the company's current situation and the reasons for having to ask the court to appoint a custodian. The letter to the bondholders stated that the semi-annual 8% interest will not be paid when it matures, and the principal and interest of the 7% bonds that are due will also be suspended.

August External Trade Deficit Exceeds 10 Million; Exports and Imports Further Decline; Trade Deficit for Eight Months This Year Exceeds 300 Million Yuan 100

The Shen Shi News Agency reports that in August, the country's external trade further declined. The import value was 56,176,344 yuan, a sharp decrease compared to 274,252,903 yuan in the same period last year and 64,376,376 yuan in the previous month. The export value was 45,331,238 yuan, also a decrease compared to 45,958,927 yuan in the previous month, but slightly increased compared to 44,057,729 yuan in the same period last year. The trade deficit significantly decreased, reaching only 10,845,106 yuan. For the eight months of this year, the total import value was 666,008,103 yuan, and the total export value was 350,659,838 yuan, both decreasing compared to the same period last year. The trade deficit was 315,348,177 yuan.

Import Values

Among the main import values in August, cotton accounted for 1,198,789 yuan, wool and its products 914,042 yuan, rayon 173,266 yuan, metals and mineral ores 2,766,091 yuan, machinery and tools 3,670,249 yuan, automobiles 310,933 yuan, miscellaneous metal products 1,679,649 yuan, rice 1,064,297 yuan, wheat 1,245,437 yuan, chemicals 1,683,386 yuan, pigments and dyes 1,519,463 yuan, and paper 1,612,584 yuan (all in Customs Gold Units).

Export Values

Consistent Promotion by All Industries; Bank Acceptance Drafts; Implementation of Acceptance Drafts Immediately Increases Leverage; Banking Industry Can Facilitate Refinancing 101

The Joint Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Banking Association is planning to establish a joint bill acceptance house to create Shanghai bank acceptance drafts. The method involves industrial and commercial enterprises in need of financing providing collateral to the house. Upon the house's approval, they can issue drafts, which the house will accept. These accepted drafts can be purchased or discounted by various banks. Those requesting acceptance can thus obtain financing. Banks, after purchasing or discounting these drafts, can still sell or rediscount them to obtain financing if they need funds themselves.

Central China and Communications Banks Handle Rediscounting

The draft plan for establishing a joint bill acceptance house and the regulations for bank acceptance drafts have both been drafted by the Joint Preparatory Committee. After discussions with banking leaders, it is generally believed that these acceptance drafts are the only effective method to increase leverage and alleviate market conditions. It is reported that the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications have agreed to handle rediscounting for these bank acceptance drafts. After implementation, the Central Bank will announce the discount rate daily. It is now decided that after the Banking Association approves, the Joint Preparatory Committee will be commissioned to prepare for its establishment.

All Industries Agree to Promote Consistently

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency, after inquiring with relevant industries yesterday, learned that the decline of Shanghai's industry and commerce has reached an extreme point. Since the silk and satin industries first created commercial acceptance drafts, the discounting of these drafts has been able to replace the current credit lending, although it is not yet widespread, it has already achieved some success. Bank acceptance drafts can replace the current chattel mortgages, and are closely related to the future revival of industry and commerce. Therefore, it is hoped that they will be implemented as soon as possible, and all industries are willing to promote them consistently. After implementation, the difficulties of the fourth and tenth months of the lunar year for industry and commerce will certainly not occur again as they have this year.

Cheng Jingsheng Continues to Report on the Disaster in Northern Jiangsu; Picheng, Tongshan, Pei County, and Feng County Affected; Picheng Suffers the Most 106

The Shanghai Fundraising Committee for Flood Relief in Various Provinces received a letter yesterday from Cheng Jingsheng, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Investigation and Relief Office, stating that he had rushed to the disaster area to survey the damage and had already telegraphed the details and the area and population of the disaster area on the seventh. Now, the severity of the disaster in the four counties is summarized and statistically presented as a percentage: (1) Picheng County suffered the most severely, with the entire territory submerged, accounting for about 47%; (2) Tongshan County, the lakeside half is a vast expanse of water, accounting for about 23%; (3) Pei County's disaster area is not as wide as Tongshan's, but the severity of the disaster exceeds it, accounting for about 20%; (4) Feng County has a narrower disaster area, accounting for about 10%.

Overview of the Central Trust Bureau's Business; Approved to Officially Open on October 1st 109

The Central Trust Bureau, after the Board of Directors of the Central Bank appointed Zhang Gongquan as Director and Zhang Nachuan as Deputy Director, has been actively preparing and has been approved to officially open on October 1st. The bureau's capital is set at 10 million yuan. An overview of its business is as follows: (1) Savings Business: (A) Civil Servant Savings: Handling savings matters for civil servants; (B) Military Savings: Handling savings matters for military personnel of the army, navy, and air force, as well as police officers; (C) Lottery Savings: Handling savings matters with periodic lottery drawings; (2) Procurement Affairs: Handling purchase matters entrusted by governments at all levels and their subordinate agencies, state-owned enterprises, or public organizations; (3) Trust Business: (A) Corporate Trust: Managing the issuance, registration, guarantee, and payment of principal and interest of state-owned and public utility bonds and stocks; (B) Deposit Trust: Handling various trust deposits for public agencies or organizations; (C) Fund Trust: Collecting, managing, and utilizing various foundation funds of public agencies or organizations; (D) Investment Trust: Managing various investment matters within the scope designated by public agencies or organizations; (E) Securities Trading: Acting as an agent for public agencies or organizations in buying and selling various securities; (F) Special Trust: Handling the inspection of publicly owned property, or entrusted investigations, designs, or liquidations for the reorganization of public and private enterprises, and other trust matters designated or approved by the government or courts; (4) Insurance Business: (A) Life Insurance: Handling life insurance matters for civil servants and military personnel; (B) Property Insurance: Handling insurance matters for publicly owned property and important documents and deeds of the government or public agencies; (5) Custody Affairs: Acting as an agent for public and private agencies or organizations in the custody of documents, deeds, securities, and materials, and collecting principal and interest of securities.

If the Italy-Ethiopia Dispute Leads to War, It Will Affect China's Export of Native Products; Non-Essential Goods Will Inevitably Be Affected 115

The Central News Agency reports that the recent dispute between Italy and Ethiopia is becoming increasingly serious. British and French fleets are concentrated in the Mediterranean, with a potential for an imminent outbreak. Regarding the impact on China's export of native products, a reporter inquired with the Shanghai Bank Investigation Office. The person in charge of the office provided the following detailed information:

War Will Disrupt Transportation

According to the person in charge, if Italy and Ethiopia inevitably go to war, and Britain is also drawn into the vortex, then the Mediterranean route will be cut off. The route from East Asia to Western Europe will either detour around the Cape of Good Hope in South Africa, or pass through the Panama Canal in the Americas, entering and exiting via the Atlantic Ocean, or pass from Vladivostok to Europe via the Siberian Railway. Transportation costs will be higher in each case. At present, neighboring countries of Britain will also be highly vigilant to prevent unforeseen circumstances. All production and consumption will lose their normal state. Consumption of non-essential goods will naturally decrease.

Sales of Peanuts and Tea Will Inevitably Decrease

China's important native products normally exported to Europe will likely be affected. The important ones are as follows: (1) Peanuts and peanut kernels: Last year, exports of peanuts and peanut kernels reached 13 million yuan, of which about 9 million yuan were transported to countries such as the Netherlands, Germany, France, Italy, Britain, Denmark, Norway, and Egypt. If war breaks out, exports will be greatly hindered, and prices may temporarily fall. (2) Tea: Last year, the export value of black tea was 12.6 million yuan, of which over 5.68 million yuan was transported to Britain, and 890,000 yuan each to the Netherlands and France. Since tea is not a necessity, consumption will inevitably decrease after the outbreak of war. Also, last year the export value of green tea was 22 million yuan, of which over 8.6 million yuan was transported to Morocco. Since Morocco is on the North African coast, located south of the Mediterranean Sea, it may be subject to blockade once war breaks out. Therefore, the future of the green tea market is not optimistic. (3) Broad beans: Last year, the export value was 1.6 million yuan, with over 1.11 million yuan transported to Italy and 840,000 yuan transported to Britain. In the future, there will be reductions and obstacles to exports. (4) Eggs: Last year, exports of eggs were 20 million yuan, with 19 million yuan transported to Britain. If the Mediterranean route is cut off this time, transportation will be more difficult. However, since eggs are a necessity in food, the impact may not be too great.

Huge Impact on Cocoon and Silk Exports

(5) Raw silk: Last year, the export value of white raw silk was over 14.43 million yuan, with 4.1 million yuan transported to France. The export value of gray raw silk was 520,000 yuan, with 420,000 yuan transported to France. The export value of yellow raw silk was 3 million yuan, with over 1.13 million yuan transported to France. Since raw silk is not a necessity, sales in France will inevitably decrease after the outbreak of war. (6) Native silk: Last year, the export value of white native silk was 510,000 yuan, with 140,000 yuan transported to Egypt. The export value of yellow silk was 3.76 million yuan, with 460,000 yuan transported to Egypt. After the outbreak of war, sales of this silk will also inevitably decrease. (7) Waste silk: Last year, exports of waste silk were 5 million yuan, with 1.53 million yuan transported to Italy, 930,000 yuan transported to France, and 630,000 yuan transported to Britain. Once war breaks out, the waste silk market will be greatly affected. (8) Cocoon silk: Last year, exports of Henan cocoon silk were 1.1 million yuan, with over 100,000 yuan transported to Egypt, France, and Germany. Last year, exports of Shandong cocoon silk were 3.3 million yuan, with 590,000 yuan transported to Britain and 170,000 yuan transported to France. If war breaks out, it will also have a considerable impact.

Carpets and Straw Mats Slightly Affected

(9) Carpets: Last year, exports of carpets were 4.84 million yuan, with 1.96 million yuan transported to Britain. Carpets are luxury goods. If war breaks out, there will also be a decrease in sales. (10) Straw braids and hat braids: Last year, exports were 1.9 million yuan, with 660,000 yuan transported to Britain and 440,000 yuan transported to France. After the outbreak of war, these straw hat braids may also be somewhat affected. In addition, although the United States is the largest market for golden grass hats, European sales are also not weak, and they may also be slightly affected after the outbreak of war. (11) Floor mats and straw mats: Last year, exports of floor mats were 1.25 million yuan, with 200,000 yuan transported to Egypt and 800,000 yuan transported to the Netherlands. Exports of straw mats were 3.93 million yuan, with 1.6 million yuan transported to Britain and 410,000 yuan transported to the Netherlands. This type of commodity will also have some impact after the outbreak of war.

Daily Necessities Will Improve

In addition, there are also metals that are sold in large quantities to Europe, but these are military necessities. If they are indispensable, they may improve after the outbreak of war. The above are all commodities that are negatively affected by the war. There are also quite a few commodities that will improve due to the war, such as cotton yarn, flour, and wheat. Generally speaking, during wartime, daily necessities often increase in price, while luxury goods tend to fall in price. Export commodities that are exclusively used by warring countries often have to fall in price, while commodities with wide sales will not be greatly affected. Subsequently, a report on the progress of negotiations in Shanghai. In addition to Ma, those who arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday included Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan and Vice Minister of Finance Zou Lin.

National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Telegraphs the Central Government Requesting the Abolition of Native Cloth Tax in Shaanxi, Gansu, and Qinghai Provinces; Various Provinces Disregard Orders and Arbitrarily Impose Taxes; Request Expedited Order for Abolition to Maintain People's Livelihood 117

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the National Government's Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry, stating (address abbreviated): We have recently received a joint telegram from the Chamber of Commerce and Farmers' Association of Anlu County, Hubei Province, which briefly states: According to a petition from farmer representatives such as Chen Tongren of this county, the land in this county is barren and agricultural production is not abundant. The livelihood of farmers relies on hand-woven native cloth, which is sold in Shaanxi, Gansu, and Qinghai provinces for relief. During the Qing Dynasty, sales were extremely high. Since the establishment of the Republic of China, various provinces along the way have levied donations and taxes on native cloth, causing sales to decline daily. When the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it was concerned about the decline of national goods and the poverty of the people. It first issued an order to all provinces to exempt taxes and donations on hand-woven native cloth, showing its painstaking efforts to promote national goods, which everyone appreciates. Unexpectedly, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Qinghai provinces disregarded the order and continued to collect taxes, and even invented special tax categories to deceive the ignorant. In 1929, representatives of the people of Anlu, together with representatives of the people of neighboring counties, jointly petitioned the Finance Department of the Hubei Provincial Government, and telegraphed the Central Executive Committee and various agencies and organizations, earnestly appealing for the abolition. The Central Executive Committee forwarded the matter to the Ministry of Finance for handling, and the Ministry of Finance approved that this native cloth was in accordance with the ministry's order and should be exempted from exchange. The provincial government issued a notice, and the ministry consulted the Shaanxi and Gansu provincial governments to follow suit. Unexpectedly, the Shaanxi and Gansu provinces turned a blind eye to the order and not only failed to exempt the original taxes but even increased them. What is particularly heavy is that a tax is added in one province and then another tax is added. For example, after taxes are added in Shaanxi and Gansu, another tax must be added when passing through Gansu. After taxes are added in Gansu, another tax must be added when passing through Qinghai. Even within one province, each region is divided, and those who pay taxes in the central region can only sell in region A. If they transfer to region B, they must pay taxes again. All kinds of repeated taxes are too numerous to list. The farmers in our county are therefore in danger of having their livelihoods cut off. Therefore, we specially petition your association to forward a request for the abolition, etc. Accordingly, we telegraphed your association to investigate and verify, and to expedite forwarding an order to the Shaanxi, Gansu, and Qinghai provinces to abide by the National Government's order of 1928 to exempt native cloth from taxes, as well as the Ministry of Finance's consultation request for tax exemption in 1929, and to immediately abolish the harsh and miscellaneous taxes and donations levied on native cloth, so that merchants can reduce costs and come to Anlu to purchase from a source, and the livelihood of Anlu farmers will not be cut off, in order to conform to the government's intention to promote national goods, and to serve as a disguised form of relief, so that the 300,000 disaster victims in Anlu will benefit immensely, etc. Approval is requested to present this telegram to your office, requesting approval to forward an order to the governments of Shaanxi, Gansu, and Qinghai provinces, ordering their subordinates to immediately abolish the taxation of native cloth, in order to facilitate the sale of native goods and maintain the people's livelihood. This is our most earnest prayer. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, respectfully bows and stamps.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegrams Request to Abolish Jiangxi Province's Collection of Tax on Domestically Produced Dyes 118

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the Jiangxi Provincial Government, requesting the suspension of the Qing Fei Shan Hou (Post-Banditry Suppression) Donation on domestically produced dyes. The original telegram is recorded below:

Telegram to the Ministry of Finance

Ministry of Finance, Nanjing: We refer to the letter from the Da Zhong Dye Factory Co., Ltd., dated the 15th of this month, which states: On August 16th, we received your association's letter No. 2950, which briefly states: We have received the Ministry of Finance's approval No. 6686, which states: We are aware that special industrial products exempt from taxes by this ministry, except for business tax, which is levied on business activities, should not be subject to other taxes and donations when passing through various places. The matters mentioned should be consulted with the governments of Jiangxi and Guangxi provinces for their information. Please be informed, etc. We have recorded the approval and sent it to you, and we hope you will take note, etc. We have recently received a shipping order from our factory, shipping fifteen pieces of Yuan Qing dye to Jiangxi via the Jiangxi Qing Fei Shan Hou Donation Bureau and Jiujiang Collection Office. We were ordered to pay taxes in the same manner as imported goods, and the price was fixed at 141 yuan per piece of Yuan Qing dye, with a 5% levy. However, the sulfurized Qing dye shipped by our factory this time is cheaper than the original powdered Yuan Qing, selling for only 20 yuan per piece. At that time, there was a formal invoice as proof, but after repeated applications, not only was tax exemption not allowed, but the market value stated on the invoice was not allowed for taxation. In this situation, the tax burden on domestically produced dyes is actually higher than that on foreign goods. Most foreign Yuan Qing dyes are worth 70 to 80 yuan, and the lowest is also above 40 yuan. As a result, the cheap domestically produced dyes are burdened with higher taxes, leading to a decline in sales in Jiangxi. Moreover, according to the content of the Ministry of Finance's approval, our factory's products are tax-exempt, and we should not be liable for provincial taxes. Today, the reality is the opposite, and it is difficult to remain silent in terms of reason and emotion. We secretly observe that foreign dye merchants are actively seeking to destroy the budding growth of our domestically produced dyes, but the government is turning a blind eye and not providing assistance, and is instead imposing pressure in an invisible way. Our factory is making every effort to appeal, but our words are light and our influence is small, and it is still difficult to correct the situation. The situation is urgent, so we specifically state our difficulties, hoping that you will review and approve, and request the Ministry of Finance to issue a clear order to all provinces that all kinds of Yuan Qing dyes with the Chinese character trademark produced by our factory, regardless of where they are sold, should not be subject to provincial taxes, in order to remove the shackles on domestically produced dyes, etc. The Chamber of Commerce has received this communication. Since the receipt of your ministry's approval, it has been more than a month, and Jiangxi Province continues to collect taxes on the company's products that have been approved for tax exemption, and deliberately inflates the price, so that the actual tax is even higher than the 5% levy on imported goods. The national policy of caring for merchants and benefiting workers is implemented in the central government, but not in the local government. This matter concerns the national foundation and the lifeblood of industry, and it is impossible to remain silent. We hereby request your ministry to review and approve, and to strictly instruct the province to order a deadline for the suspension of the tax collection, in order to comply with the original tax exemption case and safeguard the national prestige. This is for the public convenience. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully bows.

Telegram to the Jiangxi Provincial Government

Jiangxi Provincial Government, Nanchang: (Above omitted) Although your province has special circumstances in implementing the Qing Fei Shan Hou Donation, it is essentially a likin (internal transit tax). In the past, when likin was not abolished, likin was collected on ordinary goods, but likin stations also strictly complied with the law and did not force collection on items that were specially exempted from heavy taxes by order. Comparing today with the past, this minimum spirit of the rule of law should not be exceeded again. This is from the perspective of law. Porcelain is a special product of your province, and recently, because it is necessary to maintain this product, the Qing Fei Shan Hou Donation will also be suspended by the end of September this year. Therefore, although the Shan Hou Donation is generally collected on all kinds of goods, there has never been a lack of flexible measures. Yuan Qing dye is a step for our country to run its own artificial pigments, and it concerns the emerging chemical industry. The need to maintain it is no less than that of porcelain, and it should also be exempted from donations. This is from the perspective of principle. If both reasons are not adopted, then there is no reason to overvalue the price of goods that should be tax-exempt, resulting in a tax that is higher than the 5% levy on imported goods. We should request your government to order the bureau to change the tax rate according to the actual price on the invoice issued by the merchant, in order to comply with the fairness of the matter. This is for the public convenience. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully bows.

The British firm Jardine Matheson & Co., which originally operated three steamers—the Baohe, Xianghe, and Jianghe—from Shanghai to Hankou, Shashi, and Yichang, has now decided to add a new steamer, the Xinpinghe, from tomorrow to navigate the middle reaches of the Yangtze River to Yichang. General Labor Union Telegrams Guangdong Requesting Abolition of Bran Tax; Cookie Merchants' Strike Still Unresolved; Oil Workers' Livelihoods in Panic 120

Oil cake and miscellaneous grain merchants in various places have been on strike and suspended transportation to protest against Guangdong Province's imposition of a bran tax. More than a month has passed, and the situation remains deadlocked. The Shanghai General Labor Union believes that the number of oil factory workers in various places reaches more than 12,000, and their livelihoods have been greatly affected by the strike, leaving them without work to do and causing panic. Yesterday, it specially telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, requesting it to order the abolition of the bran tax and to seek a solution as soon as possible. The original telegram reads: To the esteemed Southwest Political Affairs Committee of Guangzhou: The case of the oil cake merchants in various places striking and suspending transportation to protest against the Guangdong Province's imposition of a surcharge on bran for the construction of Sun Yat-sen University has been repeatedly appealed for a halt, and various groups have telegraphed for its abolition, but no approval has been granted, resulting in a stalemate that has lasted for more than a month. The resulting long-term suspension of business has stagnated the sales of oil cakes and miscellaneous grains in various places, causing significant losses to producers, and oil factories in various places have stopped work one after another because there is no work to do, putting the livelihoods of tens of thousands of oil workers on the brink of extinction. If a solution is not sought quickly, the situation will become more serious. It has been secretly investigated that most of the oil cakes produced in various places can be used by farmers for fertilizer because they contain more nitrogen and are suitable for the southern climate. Therefore, sales to Guangdong Province account for more than 63% of the national production. It can be imagined that it is related to our country's agricultural policy. At a time when foreign fertilizers are dumped in the country, the government should encourage domestic production and reduce or exempt donations on this important agricultural raw material to facilitate sales. How can we not plan for this but instead impose surcharges, causing producers to increase costs and farmers to increase burdens, harming both production and sales? We believe that this is not possible. Therefore, we telegraphed your committee to immediately inform the Guangdong Provincial Government to abolish the surcharge on bran as soon as possible, so that merchants in various places can resume business as soon as possible, so that tens of thousands of oil workers can avoid becoming starving corpses. The telegram is extremely urgent. Zhu Xuefan, Chairman of the Shanghai General Labor Union, Standing Committee Members Li Mengnan, Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xianggao, Shao Xubai, and Long Peiyun, bow.

Ministry of Finance Explains Scope of Internal Documents; Refers to Non-Independent Capital Operations 121

Regarding the regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the implementation of the stamp tax, documents used "internally" that do not create "external rights and obligations" are exempt from stamp tax. However, how should headquarters and branch offices be interpreted? The Chamber telegraphed the Ministry of Finance for instructions. The Ministry of Finance's Tax Character No. 1213 approval states: We have received your presentation and telegram. Article 3 and other provisions of the Stamp Tax Law stipulate that all public and private organizations, whose internal documents do not create external rights and obligations, should be exempt from stamp tax. The organizations referred to in this article refer to the same organization. Warehouses, manufacturing plants, sales offices, or branches of various businesses, although there is a distinction between headquarters and branches, their capital and operations are not independent, but are actually the same organization. Therefore, documents used for mutual notification that do not create external rights and obligations can be exempted from stamping. However, some businesses have the same name for their headquarters and branch offices, but their capital and operations are completely independent, or the surface system appears to be a unified entity, but they are actually agents for others. These headquarters and branch offices each have their own rights and obligations, and the documents they use for mutual use should be subject to the provisions of Article 4 of the Stamp Tax Implementation Rules and should not be regarded as internal use. Please be informed. This is the approval.

The Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee yesterday sent separate letters to the First Special District Civic Federation, requesting them to forward the letters to the Municipal Land Bureau and the Public Concession's Works Department, and to the Second Special District Civic Federation, requesting them to forward the letters to the French Concession's Municipal Council, requesting a reassessment of land prices. (Resolved) Except for Pang Bingli, because the foreign diploma he submitted was a foreign school attendance certificate, lacking the necessary requirements for membership, and should not be admitted, the other members are approved. (15) Should we request the Ministry of Justice to pay attention to the issuance of lawyer licenses to graduates of political science departments? (Resolved) Approved. (16) (Omitted) (17) Should we send a circular to all members to carefully introduce lawyers to the association? (Resolved) Approved. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Dr. Miller Discusses the Completion of the Guangzhou Sanitarium 125

Dr. Miller, the director of the Shanghai Sanitarium, flew to Guangzhou on a Douglas-style aircraft on Tuesday of this week and returned north by plane on Thursday afternoon, landing at the Guanghua Airport. According to Dr. Miller, "The Guangzhou Sanitarium has officially opened, specializing in treating patients and teaching healthy people how to maintain their health." The completion of this hospital is very helpful in maintaining and promoting the health of the people of Guangdong. Therefore, people from all walks of life in Shanghai, Guangdong, and Hong Kong have generously donated to it. Our reporter also learned from Dr. Miller the history of the establishment of the Guangzhou Sanitarium as follows: There was a Guangzhou native, Liu Jian, who lived in California, USA. He wanted to return to his motherland to serve his poor and sick compatriots. Although he was a Christian and a member of the Seventh-day Adventist Church, he was not funded by any association. He paid his own way to enroll in a medical school in San Francisco. After graduating, he first practiced medicine in Fresno, California, and then returned to China at the invitation of the Seventh-day Adventist Church to practice medicine in Foshan, 60 miles southwest of Guangzhou. After years of hard work, he founded a well-equipped hospital there. He then opened a sanitarium in Nanning, Guangxi. After several years of development, it has now become a well-respected medical institution. When Dr. Liu was dedicating himself to serving the poor and sick, he unfortunately contracted cholera during an epidemic and tragically died within three days. However, Dr. Liu's sacrifice was not in vain, because the South China medical cause he founded has been continued by others. Two years ago, his colleagues who worked with Dr. Liu in Foshan planned to found a medical hospital in Guangzhou City. They selected a site near Dongshan and built it. After more than a year of preparation, a magnificent new-style hospital officially opened on September 25 this year. Dr. Miller, the director of the Medical Department of the China General Association of Seventh-day Adventists, said at the opening ceremony of the hospital that the association had established seven similar sanitariums in China in the past seven years, and this hospital is the most recently established one. As for its parent institution, the Shanghai Sanitarium, it was opened on January 1, 1928, at 150 Rue Pichon in Shanghai. It is said that Dr. Miller also consulted with the staff of various departments of the association in Wenzhou, Fuzhou, Xiamen, and Shantou on various plans to develop church affairs during his travels.

Far East Lumber Mill Reduces Wages 127

The Far East Lumber Mill, located on the north bank of the Suzhou Creek in Zhoujiaqiao, Shanghai West, has more than 300 workers, mostly from Shandong. The business has always been prosperous. Recently, the mill has been affected by the sluggish market, resulting in a sharp decline in business. In order to maintain operations, the mill announced at the beginning of this month that it would reduce wages. All the workers unanimously expressed their opposition and demanded that the mill withdraw its decision, but to no avail, so they went on strike. The Social Bureau has repeatedly sent personnel and Director Tan of the Caojiadu Branch Bureau and others to mediate, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched a squad of police officers and all the patrol officers from the branch bureau to maintain order and protection at the mill. More than two weeks have passed. After repeated consideration, the mill has agreed to the mediation of the Social Bureau and Director Tan and will increase each worker's wage by 25 cents. The workers have also expressed their satisfaction. Wages were paid yesterday, and work will resume as usual today.

County Government Rejects Petition of Tenants on Former County School Site; Appeal Can Be Made to the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department 132

The Ju Kui area inside the Xiaodongmen of this city is the site of the old Shanghai County School. In the year [blank], twenty households including Chen Changsheng and others leased the land from the County Public Funds and Property Office. Now that the lease term has expired, the County Education Bureau has proposed to reclaim the land. Unexpectedly, the tenants, believing that they had been deprived of their right to negotiate a renewal of the lease, elected representatives Zhu Yaoyou, Xu Jingrong, Wang Yuankai, and others to submit a petition to the Shanghai County Government, denying the County Education Bureau's claim to reclaim the land. This case has now been reviewed and decided by County Magistrate Ye. The written decision has been sent to the petitioners. The full text of the decision is as follows: (Ruling) The petition is rejected. (Reasoning) According to the rules for filing petitions, the scope should be limited to administrative actions. The petitioners in this case leased the Shanghai County School site and entered into a contract with the Local Public Property Office, which is purely a contractual relationship under private law. After the County Education Bureau took over the site, the lease contract continued to exist. When the term expired and the land was reclaimed, there was nothing improper about it. In terms of its nature, it is a claim of ownership and not an administrative action. The petitioners believe they have been deprived of their right to negotiate a renewal of the lease, and they should file a lawsuit in accordance with the law with a judicial organ. An administrative agency is not in a position to accept it. Therefore, in accordance with the first half of Article 8 of the Petition Law, the ruling is as stated in the main text. If the petitioners do not accept this ruling, they should file another petition with the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department within thirty days from the day after receiving this ruling.

New Building of HSBC Hong Kong Headquarters to Be Completed; Achievements of the Kung Ho Engineering & Architectural Co. 133

The new building of the Hong Kong headquarters of the British HSBC Bank, completed over two years, is scheduled to hold a completion ceremony on October 10th. The new building was designed by the Shanghai Kung Ho Engineering & Architectural Co. The building covers an area of 5,600 square feet. The roof is a tall tower, soaring 220 feet into the sky. The whole building is simple and solemn, made of granite, and looks very imposing. The top of the tower faces the mountain peaks in the distance. From the top of the tower, the beauty of the stone carvings of the new building can be seen. The main entrance of the bank is on Queen's Road, with a grand staircase in the middle, and staircases on both sides, one leading to the rental offices, and the other to the bank's Chinese department. Inside the main entrance is a large hall, wide and simple. The surrounding walls are made of mica stone. The huge pillars in the hall are also made of a different kind of mica stone. Above is a dome, made of Venice glass inlaid with mosaic patterns, with very beautiful colors. The floor is paved with green mica stone, surrounded by black mica stone. Above the hall is a large mica stone staircase, leading to Des Voeux Road outside. The entrance of Des Voeux Road is a large mica stone staircase. Entering the door is a small hall, from which you can access the elevator to the rental offices on the upper floors. To the left is the vault, which is separated from the bank. All methods of alarm and theft prevention are available. There are 7,000 safe deposit boxes and six safe deposit rooms. Near the main entrance of the bank is a night deposit box, for customers to deposit silver to the bank at night, to ensure safety. The Kung Ho Engineering & Architectural Co. has always built houses for HSBC. The old HSBC building in Hong Kong and the new HSBC building in Shanghai were all built by the company. In addition, buildings such as the Jianghai Customs, Sassoon House, Cathay Hotel, Kyoto Hotel, Hamilton House, and Broadway Apartments were all designed by Kung Ho. Recently, a residential area was built for China Land Company. The new building of the Bank of China was also planned by Kung Ho in conjunction with the bank's architectural staff. They are experienced and have excellent achievements. The monthly report issued by the Royal Institute of British Architects recently also recorded the achievements of Kung Ho, saying that they are rare and valuable.
