Free Talk

The Journey from Rousseau to Babbitt 219

— Wang Jicong

If Bacon is the founder of modern science, then Rousseau can be said to be the founder of modern thought that arose with the Renaissance. Rousseau's individualism and liberalism not only had a great impact on politics and general thought, but also had a great influence on literature. Rousseau himself was a literary writer, and in his general treatises and so-called argumentative novels, one can see his literary views combined with the aforementioned thoughts. He replaced the humanism of classicism with the development of individuality; he opposed the rules and rationality of classicism, advocating the liberation of emotions and allowing them to run freely. If the thought of absolutist classicism is static thought, then we can say that Rousseau's thought, which opposed classicism, is dynamic thought. He was a person who lived a dynamic and wandering life; and, according to his own account, he was also someone who believed that the body and limbs were opposed by emotions and imagination.

Such literary thought of Rousseau is, in fact, the entire ideological system of Romanticism. Many literary historians say that Rousseau is the founder of Romanticism, which is not an exaggeration. If Romanticism is a literary trend of thought produced by the emerging industrial citizens in order to break the shackles that hindered them from building their own literature, then Rousseau, the founder of Romanticism, can also be said to be the literary vanguard and the pioneer of modern literature for the industrial citizens.

However, in the eighteenth century, industrial citizens were in a period of rising prosperity. At that time, in order to obtain the right to free trade, to oppose the rule of the aristocracy, and to step onto the political stage, they actively advocated freedom and democracy, promoted individualism, and liberated emotions. The so-called Rousseau's thought is a reflection of the thought of the industrial citizens of the eighteenth century. In the nineteenth century, although there were many changes in modern citizen literature, their literature showed the development from Romanticism to Realism, but because they were still growing upward at that time, they had not fundamentally betrayed the initial thought represented by Rousseau. However, as time progressed to the twentieth century, those who do not move cannot activate their brains. He once said: "When I am in one place, I can hardly think of anything; for my mental activity, my physical activity is necessary." Therefore, he often traveled, moved, and wandered around. His whole life can be said to be a dynamic life. Combined with this dynamic life is his dynamic thought: resisting reality, opposing artificiality, advocating nature, and demanding freedom. Because he hated reality and loved nature, Rousseau also valued imagination. He was particularly critical of the rationality and rules of classicism. Especially on the eve of the Great War, modern society showed its morbidity and crisis in all aspects, and all objective facts proved that it had reached the end of the road given to it by history. Therefore, the citizens, the masters of modern society, felt that Rousseau's thought was not only useless but also harmful to them. Therefore, calls against Rousseau's thought came from all directions. Professor Babbitt's so-called humanism emerged from this.

Professor Babbitt's humanism, on the surface, seems to be a revival of classicism in the seventeenth and eighteenth centuries, but in fact it has new significance. This new significance lies in the fact that it is a product of the time around the Great War. In Professor Babbitt's view, the many dangerous social phenomena and even the brutal wars that occurred in the twentieth century were all led by Bacon's materialism and Rousseau's liberalism. Therefore, in order to avoid war and eliminate all dangerous social phenomena, he replaced the "law of matter" with the "law of human affairs," and replaced liberalism with teaching people to "follow the rules" and "not go to extremes." If people really listened to this and everyone "followed the rules" and "did not go to extremes," then the world would be peaceful and the modern society that had reached the end of its road could last forever. However, undesirable things continued to happen, and Babbitt's humanism did not show a great effect. Therefore, Professor Babbitt had no choice but to further beg for mercy from God and religion. He publicly stated that in order to maintain the status quo, he had to ask Buddha and Jesus to come out.

In literature, Professor Babbitt and his disciples completely agreed with the theory of classicism.

The literary trend of classicism existed in the seventeenth and eighteenth centuries, and Professor Babbitt's humanistic literary thought was the thought of classical righteousness; in this sense, we can say that it is a kind of retro thought. At the same time, if Rousseau was the spokesperson for the rising industrial citizens, and Babbitt's doctrine was a reflection of the thought of the citizens who had embarked on the road, then we can also say that Babbitt's doctrine is a kind of citizen thought that has developed to the final stage. Because the modern citizens who have reached the end of their road need to go back to the past and revive classicism in order to preserve their last life, so Professor Babbitt's humanism was produced. Here, there is the unity of the so-called citizen thought that has developed to the final stage and the retro thought.

Rousseau's thought is the initial citizen thought, so it is forward-looking; Babbitt's doctrine is the citizen thought that has embarked on the road to decline, so it is backward-looking. From Rousseau's thought to Professor Babbitt's humanism, it is a process of how modern citizen thought arose, developed, and declined.

A-Sheng 220

— Chu Yaming

(A girl who doesn't listen to her mother)

When I was a child, I often heard adults say two sentences that they liked to say.

"Do you want to be A-Sheng?"

"No A-Xiang, no A-Sheng!"

Why they liked these two sentences so much, as if they were an important part of a complete life, was something that I found difficult to explain at first. They judged that a girl was really bold and reckless, or naughty and mischievous, or even a little disobedient to her elders, and scolded:

"Do you want to be A-Sheng?"

Later, I finally heard the story of A-Sheng, the girl who didn't listen to her mother, from my old aunt's narration. Her expression was so reverent and solemn, as if she was talking about the legend of a god.

"Yongchang Silk Factory was the largest silk factory in Guixiang, with nine lanes in the whole factory, two boats in each lane, and fifty seats in each boat, a total of as many as nine hundred female workers." The old aunt closed her eyes and sadly described the prosperous days of the past. "As you can imagine, naturally there was a male inspector in each lane. They were used to check whether the female workers were being lazy, walking around idly all day long, talking to the female workers when they were happy. Some girls wanted to curry favor with them, some wanted to use them to relieve boredom, but some 'infected' girls didn't even look at them. However, if this was the case, they would be ashamed and angry, and would insist that you were doing rough work and immediately 'collect your cocoons' and not allow you to work. They were all afraid of those inspectors.

"The inspector in charge of the first lane was a man called Xiang-ge. One day he noticed a new young female worker who was very beautiful, and none of the female workers in the whole factory could compare to her; but she didn't say a word all day, obediently lowering her head to work. Xiang-ge patrolled around her incessantly, trying to talk to her, but seeing that she always kept her mouth shut, he became even more anxious and impatient, making the girls next to her envious and jealous. She was A-Sheng.

"A-Xiang immediately found out that A-Sheng only had a very old mother, that she was very filial to her, and listened to everything she said, and that they were very poor. A-Xiang made up his mind and went straight to her mother to discuss everything. A-Sheng herself didn't know why, but she was suddenly promoted from a junior apprentice to a second apprentice. It wasn't easy to be a first apprentice at that time, hum, she earned six dimes a day!

"On the evening of Deyang Festival, A-Sheng's mother made a table of dishes herself, bought a lot of wine, and invited A-Xiang to dinner. A-Sheng got drunk and didn't know anything. It was a bit of a sin, and her mother left A-Xiang to sleep in the same bed with A-Sheng!

"Later, when A-Sheng found out what had happened to her, she quarreled with her mother. Alas, they started fighting, and that unfilial girl injured her mother, smashing her eyes and head with something. The next day, A-Sheng abandoned her mother and fled to the provincial capital, and the following year, her mother died."

"Didn't you say that her mother was a bit sinful?" I protested.

"Sinful is sinful, what's there to say! Even if she cut her into pieces or ate her, she would still be her mother! A mother can give birth to her, so it's okay to tell her to die; besides, a mother has complete control over marriage matters."

But I knew that my old aunt was lying to me, that she must have been hiding something and didn't want to tell me, because what she said was extremely inconsistent and contradictory with the regretful and respectful expression she had when she spoke.

I ran to ask the shaman Zhong Dao-yi, who could write charms, treat illnesses, drive away ghosts, and secure families, a poor and sickly old drunkard who often ran to our door and beat our two big wooden doors or lay down in the middle of the street to sleep when he was drunk.

"Your aunt will scold me, she won't give me a single copper!"

"But why do you say 'No A-Xiang, no A-Sheng' when you encounter bad luck or someone bullies you? Do you like being A-Sheng?"

"Don't talk nonsense, you little devil!" He scolded me like this, but he was actually very happy, so he continued with his incomplete words!

"I mean, those who want to destroy my whole family, their intention to harm me may instead fulfill me. They want me to suffer losses, but they may instead let me take advantage! A-Sheng lives in everyone's heart and is immortal...

"The year after her mother died, A-Sheng, this comet, returned to Guixiang. When she left, she was a silk worker', but when she came back, she became a free woman, a female student, a queen!... No one dared to mention the past except herself. She dared to, and often brought it up in front of the old masters and local gentry, embarrassing them... At that time, they couldn't even smile in front of her... What could they do? The local self-defense army listened to her, the county magistrate often invited her to tea, she wore a horse, and ran around the streets with many men, and no one dared to provoke those men!

"At first, when A-Xiang heard that A-Sheng had come to Guixiang, he prepared to run away secretly in the middle of the night, but he didn't succeed and was escorted back by several self-defense soldiers. Those self-defense soldiers all knew about their past, and they pushed him in front of A-Sheng and said: "Sister Sheng, do you still remember him? He is A-Xiang, who used to be an inspector and is now doing housework and has a wife. Would you like to treat him to something to eat?" "Okay, let me see clearly, untie the rope!" She walked up to him; whipped him a few times with her riding crop, then told people to take him to the military court.

They sentenced him to labor, washing horses, carrying bullets, picking mulberry leaves on the mulberry field from morning till night, and the wages he earned were confiscated. A-Xiang, who was used to being pampered, couldn't stand it, and what he couldn't stand even more was that the female workers who picked mulberry leaves ridiculed their new partner all day long, singing songs and scolding him... So one night, he hanged himself in the stable.

The day after many women followed her example and paraded in white shirts and black skirts on the street, I met her. She sat in my house for a long time, talking about many things from the past... "Don't be a shaman, in the future no one will believe you and your spells, and you will slowly starve to death! Go to me and find something else to do." She said this to me and gave me a piece of paper.

"But I didn't go to her. I was a little afraid of her, and I knew that they didn't like me, or they would ask me to do hard labor, and I couldn't stand hardship even more than A-Xiang.

"But what this comet said finally came true, and now, am I not slowly starving to death? However, she said that people would not believe me, that is not right. People believe me, more than ever before, only they have no money; they can't afford to ask me to perform spells?"

Morning in the Suburbs (Part 2) 221

— Hu Yifan

In a canal with green algae, a fisherman had been submerged in the water for quite some time.

The canal was less than five or six zhang long and about two zhang wide, but it was the source of filth and dirt for the people of this village. Apart from drinking water, which they could draw buckets of muddy water from a public well without a lid or walls, they relied on this small canal for everything from washing rice and vegetables, laundering clothes, to emptying chamber pots.

At this moment, piles of people were squatting on both sides of the small canal.

Slap, slap, slap, the laundry sticks fell one after another, and the women's talk never stopped. The interesting thing was talking about A-San's divorce:

"How could A-San agree to such a thing?"

"Doesn't agree? What can A-San take to support his family?"

"He would only agree to a divorce if there was no other way to think of, right? Mother?"

"That's right. It's really hard to be a man these days. You can't find work, and there's no other way out. What can you do if your wife has an affair? If a man doesn't want to be a cuckold, a woman won't succeed if she doesn't find a way to make a living herself; that's for sure."

At this point, everyone looked at the old woman's摇头咕嘴, confident expression and stopped their hands involuntarily and laughed. However, this laughter seemed so indifferent and powerless!

"This can only be blamed on the bad market! A-San is such a diligent young man, how could he get divorced if he didn't lose his job? I heard that A-San wanted to… to… commit suicide…"

Before Yun Di's mother, with the rotten eyelids, could finish speaking, a gunshot rang out from the fence by the roadside, and the sparrows flew up in fright. Immediately, a Werther-like youth in a Western-style jacket and riding breeches appeared there, holding a red-handled black air gun, standing there arrogantly, looking around for his target.

They gasped, their chests pounding, and each of them spat lightly.

"So scary, so scary, damn animal!" The language immediately became so weak, almost inaudible.

Then there was silence. Experience told them that even young masters were coming out to take walks and hunt, so it was getting late. So they started doing their work even more frantically.

The world had obviously changed. Although this was a village and this was a morning, people had long lost their previous leisure and become more tired, and life had become more cramped.

In the fields, the songs of shepherd boys and the chants of famous scholars could no longer be heard, only sighs and cries of hardship. Even they knew: divorce, unemployment, suicide… this series of new terms!

The beginning of the day unfolded a bleak and gloomy world! (End)

Rich, bright wine, so red,

Drink it down, that

It's like the spark of life!

Take a sip,

Containing infinite bitterness,

In the gentle aftertaste.

Throw it away, no!

Sweet dreams, sour tears,

Hot passion and great strength!

A gust of wind blows from somewhere,

Sand and dust, blinding the eyes,

Tears, dripping into the clean glass,

Just like the spark of life!

I drink down the red wine!

At this time, the pastor slowly raised his head and glanced at the patient from afar: the emaciated face was covered with large black scars. Long, messy hair. The eyes were stretching upwards. The chest seemed to be still trembling slightly.

The elevator went up. The emergency room was as silent as death. Only the pale electric light reflected the crystal tears of the suicide victim, and the early autumn wind flew in from the window, blowing the white cloth on his slightly undulating chest to tremble slightly. (End)

Gonococcal Orchitis 224

— Dr. Feng Shanliang

After contracting gonorrhea, the causative agent, the gonococcus bacteria, immediately invades the urethra through the urethral opening. Initially, the gonorrhea infection is superficial, residing in the anterior urethra, where it first manifests as acute gonorrhea. At this stage, promptly taking the specific anti-gonorrhea medication "Miesha Lin" (滅殺淋) internally and applying "Lindu Shuyier" (淋毒舒藥耳) externally will swiftly eradicate the gonococcus, leading to a complete cure. However, if treatment is delayed or improperly administered, failing to eliminate the gonococcus thoroughly, the gonorrhea may not be eradicated. The gonococcus then gradually invades the posterior urethra, transitioning from subacute to chronic gonorrhea. Subsequently, it may invade the bladder, causing cystitis, or the prostate gland, leading to prostatitis, and eventually spread to the testicles, resulting in gonococcal orchitis and other associated complications of gonorrhea.

When the gonococcus invades the posterior urethra from the anterior urethra and then proceeds through the seminal colliculus and vas deferens to the testicles, causing gonococcal orchitis, the swelling of the testicles is often mistaken for a hernia (小腸氣). However, hernias are caused by the descent of the small intestine from the abdominal cavity into the scrotum, a condition medically termed "prolapse of the intestine," which is distinctly different from gonococcal orchitis. Gonococcal orchitis is solely caused by the invasion of the gonococcus into the testicles, resulting in inflammation, and is a complication of gonorrhea.

In the early stages of gonococcal orchitis, a pulling sensation is felt in the groin area. One of the testicles in the scrotum gradually develops a sensation of heaviness and swelling, accompanied by a severe, stabbing pain. The pain gradually progresses to redness and swelling, and the scrotum also becomes swollen and painful, eventually becoming significantly enlarged, sometimes more than half its original size. This makes movement difficult and walking becomes challenging. The condition may be bearable while lying down, but upon standing, it feels as if a very heavy object is hanging from the groin. Coughing exacerbates the pain, and the patient may also experience high fever and extreme fatigue. After about half a month, the redness and swelling may subside, but a hard mass will inevitably form. Once this mass forms, it cannot be eliminated quickly. Therefore, upon contracting gonorrhea, prompt treatment is crucial to eradicate the gonococcus thoroughly and prevent it from spreading to the testicles and causing severe conditions like gonococcal orchitis. This is the best course of action. (Editor's note: The Chun Zai Hospital (春在醫院) at 66 Ningbo Road in the French Concession offers highly reliable gonorrhea treatment. The hospital is equipped with comprehensive facilities, including shortwave diathermy equipment for treating gonorrhea. The fees are exceptionally low, and the results are remarkably rapid, making it a boon for gonorrhea sufferers. Furthermore, for internal gonorrhea medication, "Miesha Lin" (滅殺淋) is considered the most effective, while for external treatment, "Lindu Shuyier" (淋毒舒藥耳) is the top choice. Both are sold by Renshou Pharmacy (仁壽西藥社) at 1 Old Dexing Lane, Mintini Road. Major pharmacies like Nanyang, Wing On, and Sincere also carry these products. Gonorrhea sufferers should not miss this opportunity.)

Nocturnal Emission, Premature Ejaculation, and An Er Shen (安彌神) 225

— Dr. Cui Fuqing

Nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation are both types of neurasthenia. They are primarily caused by masturbation and excessive sexual activity. Excessive masturbation and sexual activity deplete the body of semen, causing excessive consumption and a decline in endocrine fluids, which leads to neurasthenia. This results in conditions like nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation, which develop gradually. The reason for this is that the nervous system governing sexual desire and the central nervous system become highly sensitive and easily stimulated, leading to the rapid ejaculation of semen, resulting in nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation. Human semen is extremely precious, originating from the testicles. Through the function of the epididymis, it enters the seminal vesicle walls via the vas deferens. A portion flows into the lymphatic vessels and then into the blood vessels, circulating in the bloodstream as nourishment. Another portion returns to the testicles via the arteries, reforming into semen and completing the semen circulation. Excessive nocturnal emission, masturbation, and sexual activity all deplete semen. The physiological production of new blood cannot replenish the loss, gradually depleting the brain, spinal cord, and nervous system, leading to neurasthenia and subsequently premature ejaculation, as well as various other diseases caused by this condition, such as brain diseases, stomach diseases, sexual organ diseases, and heart diseases. Therefore, nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation can be the root cause of various diseases, potentially endangering life and should not be ignored. The causes of nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation are primarily excessive discharge leading to insufficient nourishment of the nervous system, reproductive organs, and endocrine system. The treatment method should focus on supplementing the body's endocrine fluids and replenishing essential substances for the nervous system, particularly phosphorus. "An Er Shen" (安爾神) is a highly reliable endocrine phosphorus preparation that has a special and remarkable effect on the treatment of neurasthenia and is also an effective medicine for treating nocturnal emission and premature ejaculation.

Female Infertility and Gonorrhea 226

— Liu Xuan

Female infertility can be divided into two categories: infertility due to natural physiological defects and infertility due to illness. Infertility due to physiological defects is rare, with most cases being due to illness. There are various causes of female infertility, but infertility caused by gonorrhea is the most common and prevalent. Medical studies have shown that gonorrhea accounts for 60-70% of female infertility cases. Therefore, gonorrhea has a significant impact on female fertility.

In men, the gonococcus initially invades the urethra. In women, it first invades the vaginal cavity and uterus. When the gonococcus invades the vaginal cavity, it causes vaginitis. After invading the uterus, it inevitably causes endometritis and metritis, which often lead to infertility. Gonorrhea can also cause changes in the position of the uterus, which is a major cause of infertility.

In women with gonorrhea, the gonococcus can spread from the uterus to the fallopian tubes, causing salpingitis and abscesses. The fallopian tubes may even become completely blocked, leading to absolute infertility. Further progression to the ovaries can cause oophoritis, hindering egg maturation and preventing ovulation, which also leads to infertility. Additionally, gonorrhea can cause tumors in the uterus, ovaries, and fallopian tubes, as well as changes in the position of the uterus, all of which can lead to female infertility. Another major cause of infertility in women with gonorrhea is that the activity of sperm ejaculated by men is destroyed by the gonococcus in the vaginal cavity, naturally leading to infertility. Therefore, if gonorrhea in women is not cured, it will inevitably hinder fertility and cut off the family line, which is a matter of great importance.

If a woman contracts gonorrhea but the gonococcus has not yet deeply invaded the uterus, external treatment with "Lindu Shuyier" (淋毒舒樂耳) can completely eliminate the gonococcus in the vaginal cavity. If the gonococcus has invaded the uterus, internal medication with "Miesha Lin" (滅殺淋) should be used as the primary treatment to eradicate the gonococcus and cure the gonorrhea, preventing it from leading to infertility.

Talking About Tinea 227

— Dr. Sun Zhiyao

Tinea is a skin disease that is highly contagious. Patients often experience recurring episodes. Without effective dermatological medications, it is extremely difficult to eradicate. The source of tinea is usually through transmission. Professionals such as doctors and nurses, due to the nature of their work, have frequent skin contact with patients, making them susceptible to transmission. Privileged individuals with weakened skin resistance are also prone to transmission. Farmers exposed to sun and rain are susceptible to skin diseases of the head and face. Butchers and shepherds who come into contact with livestock often develop ringworm. Carpenters and shoemakers, who constantly work with calluses, are prone to rashes or eczema. Those living on the water, due to constant exposure to moisture, are particularly prone to various stubborn tineas.

Diet also has a close relationship with tinea. People who enjoy drinking alcohol are more likely to develop "wine tinea." Those who consume spicy foods are also more prone to tinea.

Climate also plays a role in tinea. In humid and hot regions, eczema and miliaria are prevalent in spring and autumn. In winter, lichen simplex chronicus and prurigo nodularis are common. In summer, pityriasis versicolor, rashes, and tinea versicolor are prevalent. Other types of tinea, such as ichthyosis and keratoderma, are not only infectious but also hereditary.

Age also affects the type of tinea that develops. Tinea in children is often characterized by pigmented measles, ichthyosis, and other conditions. Middle-aged individuals are more prone to intertrigo and athlete's foot. Elderly individuals are more likely to develop seborrheic keratosis and epithelioma. The type of tinea varies with age.

In addition to the above, there are countless types of stubborn tinea. However, the cause is always transmission. All types of tinea are caused by the invasion of microorganisms into the skin. Once these microorganisms are transmitted, tinea immediately develops. This is why tinea is so contagious and difficult to eradicate. Only by completely eliminating the microorganisms can the condition be cured. Current treatment methods using artificial sunlamps and quartz mercury lamps have surprisingly effective results. For external medication, "Jiejue Jun" (潔絕菌), sold by Renshou Pharmacy (仁壽西藥社) on Old Dexing Lane, Mintini Road, is considered the best. It can treat various stubborn tineas and effectively eliminate tinea.

The Scope and Miraculous Effects of "Wei Bao" (胃寶) in Treating Stomach Disorders 228

— Dr. Cui Zhongbin

Stomach disorders are not limited to the stomach itself. Many symptoms can be related to the stomach, causing stomach pain. However, most stomach pain is caused by stomach disorders. Stomach pain caused by gastric ulcers and duodenal ulcers is closely related to diet. The pain occurs when hungry and can be alleviated by eating a reasonable amount of food. The pain comes and goes. In addition to pain, there are often symptoms such as hematemesis, acid reflux, and black stools. This type of stomach disorder is the most common.

Some stomach pain is caused by neurasthenia and is a type of neurotic stomach pain. There are no ulcers in the stomach. The pain can be very severe. This is also a type of stomach disorder. Stomach cancer is also a stomach disorder. It is very difficult to treat and can be life-threatening. However, if detected early, it is not an incurable disease. Stomach pain caused by stomach cancer is usually continuous. The pain occurs when hungry and when full. Sometimes, a hard mass can be felt in the stomach. This type of stomach disorder is the most dangerous.

Other diseases such as cholecystitis and acute gastritis can also cause stomach pain. However, the location and nature of the pain vary.

Opium and the Human Body 231

— Physician She Lei

Prolonged use of morphine or opium, either as medication or as a habit, will gradually lead to addiction. Eventually, tolerance develops, and only a large dose can be effective. The most addictive method is subcutaneous injection of morphine, followed by smoking opium with a lamp. The reason why people develop tolerance to large doses of morphine or opium is that their bodies become more efficient at breaking down morphine. At the same time, the functions of various organs change to counteract the effects of morphine. Animal experiments have shown that animals accustomed to morphine have a more active morphine-degrading mechanism, even to the point where the amount of morphine excreted in its original form decreases. At this point, the animal desires morphine greatly and enters a morphine-dependent state. The more it consumes, the greater its tolerance becomes, and its craving for morphine intensifies. Over time, various health problems gradually develop, leading to chronic morphine poisoning. At this point, the visible symptoms include decreased saliva secretion, increased sweating, constricted pupils, extreme emaciation, loose skin, and digestive disorders. Initially, there is stubborn constipation, followed by diarrhea, leading to physical and mental exhaustion. The person experiences dizziness, headache, tremors in the limbs, neuralgia, insomnia, and eventually dementia and paralysis. Needless to say, for these patients, even those who have not reached this stage but are already accustomed to morphine, suddenly stopping their morphine or opium supply will trigger withdrawal symptoms. Approximately several hours after cessation, symptoms such as chills, yawning, headache, severe neuralgia, diarrhea, vomiting, and insomnia will appear. Among these, insomnia can last for several days. In more severe cases of withdrawal, the patient initially presents with manic behavior, followed by hallucinations and tremors, eventually developing full-blown psychosis. The most terrifying aspect of withdrawal is collapse, which can lead to death.

Is Bertrand Russell a Supporter of Social Darwinism? 232

— Meng Ruo

Paris, 19th, National Telegram: Bertrand Russell, the world-renowned political, social, economic, and philosophical thinker, told the Associated Press today that the United States cannot avoid being drawn into any European war, and that he greatly appreciates the United States' policy of seeking neutrality. However, he said that he does not believe this plan will work in the event of a war, such as the last World War, the United States initially tried to strictly maintain neutrality, but it was ineffective, because there are economic factors that make it difficult for the United States to stay out of the matter. What Italy is doing today is certainly perverse, and what Britain is doing is also very foolish. Britain should not be so strongly opposed to Italy. We must assess the facts, and we should know that Abyssinia, when viewed by Europe and the world, is not important. In the event that the war spreads, Europe and the world will be affected. For the sake of the world, it seems that we should reluctantly agree, and if necessary, we should not hesitate to sacrifice Abyssinia.

The Italo-Abyssinian issue has reached a dangerous point at the current stage. It is foreseeable that Mussolini may not accept the recommendations made by the Five-Nation Committee of the League of Nations, and is determined to implement his original intention to conquer Abyssinia. Therefore, the situation in East Africa, unless King Haile Selassie gives in, I am afraid there is no hope of a clear solution. Let us set this aside for the time being. However, we feel that after the outbreak of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, most countries in the world have disapproved of Italy's barbarity and bullying, and sympathize with Abyssinia. In particular, a group of small and weak nations have expressed their displeasure for Abyssinia, and have given Abyssinia a lot of spiritual support. Mr. Russell, who is known as a great thinker and scholar of his generation, has actually made such a remark, which really makes people dare not believe that there is any morality and justice in the world. Is Mr. Russell a supporter of Social Darwinism?

According to Russell's views, the purpose is nothing more than to avoid the expansion of the war, and the intention is not necessarily bad. Naturally, when we assess the facts, Abyssinia is not important when viewed by Europe and the world, which is obvious. If Britain so strongly opposes Italy, in the event that the war spreads, Europe and the world will be affected. Therefore, for the sake of world security, not only should we reluctantly agree, but when it is absolutely necessary, we should not hesitate to sacrifice Abyssinia. Sacrificing Abyssinia is only sacrificing an unimportant country. If the war is allowed to expand, it will have a significant impact on the overall situation in the world. To resolve the Italo-Abyssinian issue, this is the most straightforward and quick solution, which is more clever and easier to implement than the plans proposed by the Three-Nation Conference and the League of Nations Conference. Mussolini, upon hearing this, will surely consider Russell as a comrade, applaud and exclaim, "It really suits my heart." However, the weak and small nations of the world will have no room to survive in the future.

We believe that the best way to eliminate world disputes is to stop the aggressive behavior of the strong. If we are only capable of sacrificing weak countries, it will only lead to greater chaos. Most of the international incidents arise from the strong seeking gains from the weak. Without the strong oppressing the weak, the peaceful world will rarely be disturbed. Everyone can see this fact clearly. For example, today's Italo-Abyssinian dispute, how did it arise? Is it Italy's unreasonableness, or Abyssinia's fault? To resolve this issue, sacrificing Abyssinia can indeed satisfy Italy's demands and temporarily prevent it from affecting the overall situation. However, the world in the future will have no justice to speak of. Whoever has the power can act recklessly in the world. Weak and small nations are only fit to be slaughtered. In this case, how can world peace be maintained? This is probably something that even the great thinker and scholar Bertrand Russell cannot answer.

Birthday 233

— Si Quan

In the morning, upon rising, on my writing desk, in the purple clay vase, was a bunch of blooming crimson dahlias. The scattered newspapers and magazines on the desk were all neatly cleaned up. The gentle September sunlight streamed through the window screen and onto the desk. This small desk, usually a cat's nest that gave one a headache just looking at it, appeared so harmonious and beautiful today, so endearing.

I am fond of flowers and plants, but after coming to Shanghai, firstly, I was too busy with work and had no leisure for such things which outsiders might consider refined. Moreover, there was really no place to grow flowers in the cramped apartments where every inch of land was precious. However, I would occasionally buy a bunch to decorate the place when passing by a flower shop. I also have a strange quirk: I don't like flowers with strong fragrances. I prefer those with vivid colors and a faint fragrance, which is why I particularly like big flowers.

I'm planning to move house soon due to a job change, so I've become very lazy. Not only is my writing desk messy, but every corner of the room is filled with stuff. But when I looked away from the purple clay vase, I found that the room was a little tidier today. Perhaps my wife couldn't stand the dirtiness and took the trouble to spend some time cleaning up, I thought.

My wife heard me getting up and came upstairs. She pretended to be angry and said, "Lazybones, you always make it look like a pigsty a few days before moving. What will people think if friends come over?" Seeing that I was just standing there, not even washing my face, she changed her tone and said with a smile, "Hurry up and wash your face, then invite some friends over for noodles."

"Why?" I was surprised. Last night, my wife told me that we didn't even have enough money for the moving expenses. How could she be so extravagant as to invite guests today?

"It's your birthday today! You're thirty years old, and you don't even know your own birthday!"

When I heard this, I wanted to laugh, but seeing how excited my wife was, how she had spent the whole morning cleaning the room and tidying up the writing desk for my thirtieth birthday, and how she remembered that last year on this day, some friends happily came to our house for noodles. They said that Shanghai people celebrate the year ending in nine, so they were celebrating my birthday in advance. I wasn't particularly excited, but it wouldn't hurt to have a bowl of noodles. Twenty-nine or thirty years old...

Page 18

But my wife thought that thirty was a significant birthday. Last year, she invited friends over for noodles, so what would it look like if it was so quiet this year? Not wanting to disappoint her, I ended up inviting a few friends over, and we had a happy day.

Fabricating a reason, I took a day off, considering it my thirtieth birthday. Now it's midnight, everything is quiet, and I'm sitting in front of my writing desk, gazing at the bunch of dahlias. I feel that a woman's love for her husband is all-encompassing, and that a person's birthday is a momentous occasion in their eyes. In reality, living to thirty or forty is merely a record of the time one has spent in the world. What is there to commemorate? I never remember my birthday, although when I was a child, I could wear new clothes for a day and remembered the day I was born very well. Now, the burden of the family rests on my shoulders, and I'm constantly calculating living expenses. When I think about how many days I've lived, it's actually a painful memory! But still, I am thirty years old. According to the average lifespan, I've only lived half my life. There are so many more birthdays to come. But how will I spend each of the remaining days? Perhaps like those dahlias, which are now blooming so brightly, but whose lives will be immediately taken by the purple clay vase. Maybe they'll be thrown into the garbage before I even move. Isn't human life just as fleeting? Then why bother remembering one's birthday?

Hometown 234

— Jiang Da

Main Street

After a war and years of disasters, Main Street was clearly in decline, devoid of vitality. When I returned home a few years ago, it was still the most bustling street in the entire city. Shopkeepers were busy with their business all day long. People going to and from the countryside carried loads of goods, and pedestrians filled the narrow road like ants. From dawn to dusk, there was hardly a moment of quiet. But now, everything had changed. Even the mornings, which used to be the busiest, saw only a few people walking around. By afternoon, it was so quiet that even the sound of a hungry dog passing by seemed unusually loud. The doors of the shops were covered with a thick layer of dust, as if they hadn't been opened in years. The goods on the shelves looked like unsold old stock, covered in dust. The shopkeepers were listlessly dozing off. All of this showed that Main Street was completely different. Perhaps the people of the hometown had seen this for so long that they found it normal. But for someone like me, who hadn't returned home in years, it was shocking. Even though Wen Di had already told me on the way back to my hometown: "The hometown is no longer the hometown it used to be."

In Front of the Guan Yu Temple

Going straight to the end of Main Street was the temple of Lord Guan Yu, considered the most efficacious in the entire city. It left a deep impression on me as a child because it was the liveliest and most fun place in the city. There were people gambling on "fish, shrimp, and crab," "twelve characters," and "four colors." There were also opera performances, storytelling, street performers doing magic tricks, and martial arts demonstrations. All sorts of entertainment gathered there, and because there were so many things to do, the place was always lively. Businesswomen would also stroll around there at night. So, anyone who had been to my hometown had almost certainly visited the Guan Yu Temple. As a child, I played there every day. Therefore, even though many years have passed, I still remember it clearly. Especially during the New Year and festivals, it was even more crowded. Merchants set up stalls, and groups of men and women from the city and the countryside came to offer incense. The temple keeper's income during these times of the year was considerable. So, every time I met the old temple keeper, he was always smiling. But now, the Guan Yu Temple in front of me had changed. The roof and the two fire doors in front of the temple used to be painted in dazzling red and gold, the walls were bright white, the red-faced Lord Guan was adorned with gold powder and wore a bright red robe every year, and the stone incense burner in front of the seat was always filled with thick smoke. All of that was gone. There were small bullet holes on the corners of the temple roof, the two main doors were missing, the walls were stained with large patches of black from rainwater leaks, the three stone incense burners were chipped and covered in spiderwebs, and Lord Guan in the seat looked older, his face covered in a layer of gray-black dust. Everything was different from the past. Under the screen wall, where gambling stalls used to be covered with white cloths, there were now only a few stalls laid out sparsely on the ground. The gamblers were just a few people wearing shorts or worn-out long gowns, and "twelve characters" had become "fan-tan." Moreover, I discovered that Old Wu from Wu Cuo Cheng, who used to be very honest and law-abiding, was in the crowd, pointing and gesticulating while discussing gambling strategies. His wrinkled face suddenly flushed red. He approached me and asked when I had returned, then lowered his head embarrassedly and said, "I'll come see you tonight," before quickly walking away.

Hometown, the hometown of my childhood, the hometown of the golden age, everything has passed. What stands before me is this desolate ancient city!

Mosquitoes 235

— Er He

In recent years, since I embraced the city life, I only suffered from the misery of bedbugs and forgot the ferocity of mosquitoes. This time, after returning to the fiery old home in June and staying there until after the bleak Mid-Autumn Festival before returning to Shanghai, I have deeply felt the hatred of mosquitoes. Zhuangzi's "Heavenly Movement" says, "Mosquitoes are fond of fine dust, causing sleepless nights." I have experienced this pain firsthand.

I never imagined that these gray, long-legged little things could be so ferocious. Although mosquitoes have always existed, I feel somewhat like Mrs. Jiu Jin, feeling that the mosquitoes of today are indeed different from the mosquitoes of the past. I clearly remember that the mosquitoes of the past were dull-witted, and it was very easy to kill ten or twenty of them. But the mosquitoes of today seem to have particularly keen senses. By the time I feel the sting and want to kill them, they have already flown away. Perhaps this is due to my old age.

This year, the harvest in the countryside is not bad, but there are especially many mosquitoes, which coincides with a well-known saying among the old and young in the countryside: "Many flies in a famine year, many mosquitoes in a harvest year." This means that many flies indicate a famine year, and many mosquitoes indicate a harvest year. This year, there are very few flies in the countryside, almost none. Although this is unfounded, the saying "Many flies in a famine year, many mosquitoes in a harvest year" does indeed apply to this year. However, I am the one who suffers from this. In fact, I have suffered enough because of mosquitoes.

Ancient books say: "Flies form a market in the morning, mosquitoes form a market in the evening." Indeed, there are particularly many mosquitoes in the evening, their momentum is vast, worthy of being called a "market." I live alone in a room that is not very big and not very small. I spend the whole day sweating in a wicker chair. Of course, I can't read, but the mosquitoes keep bothering me, preventing me from even having a moment of quiet fantasy. This makes me very sad. I have no choice but to hide inside the mosquito net. Because I got a moment of peace, I recalled a fantasy from four years ago. At that time, I imagined that I was a mosquito, and I could break into embroidered boudoirs and steal into silk curtains to suck the blood of beautiful young ladies. Even if I were killed, it could be said that I was "dying for love." But now, my mood is old after all, and these wild fantasies can no longer capture me! I feel the pain of a prisoner. Sweating, I lift the mosquito net and lie back on the wicker chair. But the mosquitoes still don't let me go. If it were in the past, I would have thought of various methods of revenge. I once painstakingly killed more than three hundred mosquitoes at once. It was a summer night, and because I was too tired, I fell asleep early. But I accidentally pushed the mosquito net open, and four or five mosquitoes came to visit me. Because I was tired, I ignored them. But they kept coming in larger and larger numbers, making it impossible to fall asleep. I woke up and decided to kill the mosquitoes to my heart's content. So, I simply pushed the mosquito net open, kept slapping everywhere, and waited quietly for the mosquitoes to come in. Finally, I tightened the mosquito net again, lit the lamp, and patiently scalded them. In this battle, I killed more than three hundred mosquitoes, none escaped. I felt victorious, turned off the light, and fell asleep soundly. But now, I have no intention of arguing with the mosquitoes. Sometimes, I stare blankly like a bookworm at the mosquitoes feasting on my blood, some flying clumsily like they are dragging "red lanterns," unable to fly, and some flying lightly like swallows, up and down. Then I hum: "When full, cherries are heavy; when hungry, willow catkins are light." I even forget the pain.

The reason I don't kill mosquitoes is not because I want to learn from the filial son Wu Meng of the Jin Dynasty, who did not drive away mosquitoes in the summer, fearing that they would leave him and bite his parents. I am simply too lazy to move. But after all, there is the pain of being bitten, and sometimes I unexpectedly kill two or three of them. Thinking of Meng Dongye's line, "Just seeking blood to fill, feeling life is cheap," I feel deeply saddened by the mosquitoes.

Around the Mid-Autumn Festival, the mosquitoes were probably more relentless because their death was approaching, making me suffer particularly severely. Now I have drifted back to the city. Based on past experience, I may not return to my hometown in three or four years. This rough article carries a bit of sadness.

Miscellaneous Notes from a Mountain Residence 236

— Meng Hua

(1) Autumn Rain

Autumn, in the northern country, is the season of rain.

Page 19

Page 20

Page 21

I live alone in this remote mountain village, and the days are already difficult to pass. If I also encounter rainy days, the boredom is even more unimaginable.

At night, before going to bed, I always push open the window and look to see if there are any glittering stars in the sky. I am so afraid of rainy days. When I see the sky and earth merging into a boundless darkness, my heart sinks, and I fear that tomorrow will be a rainy day. Several times, I even dreamed of being caught in a heavy rain in the mountains.

Waking up early in the morning, seeing the sky outside the window a vast expanse of blue, as clear as jade in the imperial palace, and the sun like a soft tentacle, gently stroking the high wall across from me, I happily jumped out of bed, took my cane, and walked up the hillside to see the autumn forest and fields shrouded in a light veil. But autumn is the rainy season in the northern country, and it doesn't give me, this sick person, many sunny days. It's either heavy shade or drizzle.

Once, it rained for nearly ten days straight. The only pastime in the mountain residence was originally walking, but the mountain roads were full of yellow mud, and even after the rain, it was difficult to walk without slipping. So, I had to stay in the house all day, silently watching the rain leaking through the small thatched roof, watching the small splashes of water falling on the ground. Otherwise, I would lean against the damp windowsill, watching the reeds by the water's edge weeping and whispering in the wind and rain, or the small streams pouring down the hillside, and the blurred mountains and fields shrouded in thick smoke. At this time, my mood is depressed. I also often think about how much this humid air is ruining the health of this sick person. (To be continued)

Mourning cries everywhere, wounds filling the horizon, the enemy's cannons shake the sky, and the blood of compatriots stains the desolate field, destroying cities and villages, separating children from parents and grandparents! Wandering all over the world, wandering, where is our hometown?

Ballad Singing 239

Xing Ruiting's Hairpin Phoenix

Huiling (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening "Receiving News"

A small boat turns and returns to the home mountain. Fully loaded and returning with great wealth. I only worry, Tang Shi is still without news. If Zhao Rong comes again, how will I arrange it? I might as well go to the Tang family first. After thinking it over, I come out of the door. Leading the servant boy all the way around the long street. Walking to the side of Botong Bridge. I meet a boatman and bump into him. I ask him why he's so busy. Mi Tian Gong smiles and starts talking. He says that on the day before the Mid-Autumn Festival last year. He met Tang Sheng at the corner of the water. He calls a small boat and follows the big boat closely. He was kindly allowed to paint a hundred pieces of frost white silk. So, I've been coming to Tao Wu every day to look for news. The speaker is unintentional, but the listener is mindful. Zhishan's team is exceptionally happy. I give the boatman a gift of money first. The main planner is in my heart. I hate Zhao Rong for believing the family servant's words. She shouldn't have, she used force in my hall. Today's repayment is not difficult. I happened to meet Hengshan and his companions. They say that Tang Yin has already gone to the springs. The eight concubines all cried bitterly. Yunming hurriedly put on a smiling face. Fang will tell the whole story. The crowd of beautiful women are surprised, happy and suspicious. Although the information is conveyed, the person is not seen. I don't know when the flowers will be brought back. I beg them to go to Liting together. I persuade the good man to return to Su Tai early. Husband and wife can avoid separating.

News

The Roman Art Society will broadcast a children's program in Shanghai dialect "Stutter" entitled "The Final Victory" at Li Shude Hall this Sunday afternoon, meaning to call on the weak who are oppressed by the strong to unite and resist. Little friends who care about the country, please pay special attention, and recruit young male and female members under the age of fifteen, who only need to be able to speak Mandarin or sing in school. Those who are interested should write to the society's office at No. 19, Renhua Lane, Sapore Road, just write your name, age, gender, school status, skills and mailing address, it is best to send a small photo, those who pass the test will receive a letter, deadline is October 5th.

Movie News

Silver Jottings 241

— Zhi Er

Under Mr. Zhao Banglu's strategy, Diantong has issued back pay. The news of the issuance of back pay naturally caused a thunderous cheer among the small clerks who had been hoping for rain after a long drought, but when the back pay was actually issued, it was a post-dated check for the next month, so the small clerks seemed to have to tighten their belts and wait for the date on the check to arrive.

I hope this is not a bounced check!

It is expected that after a month, Bao Ke "generation" will definitely borrow the power of Yuan (Muzhi) and Zhao (Bang...?) to promote Diantong's propaganda department.

Shang Boxun will go to Xi'an to become a movie theater owner.

After the rehearsal of "Xi Shi," someone said: China has such a beautiful woman, that's good one; a beauty who can save the country, that's good two; and now we can actually see such a play, that's good three.

In addition to these three goods, perhaps it should be added another good; such a good play is directed by Chen Dabei Guangsheng, that is good four. (Even with Mr. Chen Gexin's music direction, that is good five.)

Xu Qinfang and her Beloved Daughter 242

— Du Ao Photography

Introduction to "Night Fragrance" 243

Script

"Night Fragrance" is directed by Cheng Bugao and has been in production for over a year. It was temporarily suspended for several months due to Ms. Hu Die's departure from the country. Now that Hu Die has returned, the entire project has been completed through day and night efforts and is presented to the public. The film is a love tragedy, with the main characters being a flower girl played by Hu Die, a young worker played by Zhao Dan, and a village girl played by Shu Xiuwen, forming a love triangle—Zhao Dan is deeply in love with Hu Die, while Shu Xiuwen is infatuated with Zhao Dan. Later, Hu Die is seduced by the young master Sun Min. Zhao Dan, heartbroken, angrily and resolutely marries Shu Xiuwen. In the end, Hu Die is abandoned by the young master Sun Min, Shu Xiuwen tragically dies in the chaos of war, and Zhao Dan sacrifices his own life for Hu Die. Here is an excerpt of what the director, Bugao, said about the script: "The script for 'Night Fragrance' was planned with Chen Jun Shouyin six or seven years ago. I also discussed it with Huang Jun Zibu the year before last, and finally last year, the old idea was revisited, new materials were sought, and with the enthusiastic help of friends, the play was completed."

Director

Director Cheng Bugao has a long history and significant contributions in China. The release of "Spring Silkworms" and "Raging Tides" marked a new era for Chinese cinema, rescuing it from the sentimentality of the Mandarin Ducks and Butterfly School and setting it on a new path. "Night Fragrance" is the culmination of his efforts over the past six or seven years. He had already planned to make this film when "Raging Tides" and "Spring Silkworms" were released. It can be said that "Night Fragrance" is his masterpiece following "Raging Tides" and "Spring Silkworms."

Actors

Hu Die: Needless to say, her acting skills have reached a state of perfection. She can play any type of character perfectly. The release of "Twin Sisters" demonstrated her acting ability and talent. In the same scene, she portrayed the archetypes of two different classes, rich and poor. The poor and humble expression of "Da Bao" and the luxurious demeanor of "Bao" are probably deeply imprinted in the minds of the audience, right? "Night Fragrance" is her commemorative work from her European tour, and of course, it is also a work in which she put extra effort into her acting.

Zhao Dan: Is a talented actor. Although his history of transitioning from stage to screen is not long, and he has not starred in many films, his name has already spread throughout the Chinese film industry. The characters he plays on screen are often very sentimental. In "Night Fragrance," he still plays a very neurotic person, but this time it is not the intellectual he is used to playing, but a passionate peasant youth. Undoubtedly, he will present a new image to us.

Sun Min: Is known for playing frivolous young masters. We know that playing a "villain" is more difficult than playing a "hero." The reason is that the "villain's" actions and attitudes are almost always repulsive. Actors often confuse "frivolity" with cunning and "superficiality" with "insidiousness," and cannot distinguish between them clearly. On the other hand, the scriptwriters often arrange many sympathetic plots for the "hero," making it easier to win the audience's favor. Sun Min still plays a frivolous young man in "Night Fragrance." His "cunning" actions on screen are almost unrecognizable from his usual self. Friends who know him do not believe that the superficial villain in "Night Fragrance" is the docile Sun Min. According to people who have seen the preview of "Night Fragrance," Sun Min is much more successful in this role than in his previous films.

Shu Xiuwen: Is also an actress who transitioned from stage to screen like Zhao Dan. She has not acted in many plays, but we can fully see her talent. In "Hot-Blooded Loyal Souls," she played the role of Qiu Jin. The expression and attitude of a pre-Qing revolutionary youth dissatisfied with the Manchus, as well as Qiu Jin's personality, were clearly expressed by her, giving people a full sense of realism. In "Night Fragrance," she plays a mean older sister who is infatuated with Zhao Dan and jealous of Hu Die, trying every means to destroy her rival in love. When she discovers that Hu Die is having an affair with Sun Min, she immediately tells Hu Die's father and Zhao Dan, making them both angry. She cunningly provokes Hu Die's father on the one hand, and comforts Meisheng on the other. With her cleverness, playing such a clever character is sure to be a success.
